<script>
    let currentEditId = null;

    // åŠ è½½è´¦å·åˆ—è¡¨
    async function loadAccounts() {
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/fallback-accounts');
            const data = await res.json();
            const container = document.getElementById('accountsList');

            if (!data.accounts || data.accounts.length === 0) {
                container.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-full text-center py-8 text-slate-400">æš‚æ— æ•°æ®</div>';
                return;
            }

            container.innerHTML = data.accounts.map(acc => `
                <div class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm p-6 border border-slate-200 hover:shadow-md transition">
                    <div class="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
                        <h3 class="text-lg font-bold text-slate-900">${acc.username || 'æœªè®¾ç½®'}</h3>
                        <span class="px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold ${acc.is_active ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700' : 'bg-red-100 text-red-700'}">
                            ${acc.is_active ? 'âœ… å¯ç”¨' : 'âŒ åœç”¨'}
                        </span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="space-y-2 text-sm text-slate-600">
                        <div class="flex items-center">
                            <i class="ti ti-id mr-2"></i>
                            <span>ID: ${acc.id}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="flex items-center">
                            <i class="ti ti-link mr-2"></i>
                            <a href="${acc.group_link || '#'}" target="_blank" class="text-indigo-600 hover:underline truncate">
                                ${acc.group_link || 'æœªè®¾ç½®ç¾¤ç»„é“¾æ¥'}
                            </a>
                        </div>
                        <div class="flex items-center">
                            <i class="ti ti-coin mr-2"></i>
                            <span>ç´¯è®¡æ”¶ç›Š: ${acc.total_earned || 0} U</span>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mt-4 flex space-x-2">
                        <button onclick="editAccount(${acc.id}, '${(acc.username || '').replace(/'/g, "\\'")}', '${(acc.group_link || '').replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')" class="px-3 py-1.5 text-sm bg-slate-100 hover:bg-slate-200 text-slate-700 rounded-lg transition-colors">
                            ç¼–è¾‘
                        </button>
                        <button onclick="toggleAccountStatus(${acc.id}, ${acc.is_active ? 'false' : 'true'})" class="px-3 py-1.5 text-sm ${acc.is_active ? 'bg-red-50 hover:bg-red-100 text-red-600' : 'bg-green-50 hover:bg-green-100 text-green-600'} rounded-lg transition-colors">
                            ${acc.is_active ? 'åœç”¨' : 'å¯ç”¨'}
                        </button>
                        <button onclick="deleteAccount(${acc.id})" class="px-3 py-1.5 text-sm bg-red-50 hover:bg-red-100 text-red-600 rounded-lg transition-colors">
                            åˆ é™¤
                        </button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('åŠ è½½è´¦å·å¤±è´¥:', error);
            showToast('é”™è¯¯', 'åŠ è½½è´¦å·å¤±è´¥: ' + error.message, 'error');
        }
    }

    // æ˜¾ç¤ºæ·»åŠ è´¦å·æ¨¡æ€æ¡†
    function showAddAccountModal() {
        currentEditId = null;
        document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = 'æ·»åŠ æ¡æ¼è´¦å·';
        document.getElementById('usernameInput').value = '';
        document.getElementById('groupLinkInput').value = '';
        document.getElementById('accountModal').classList.remove('hidden');
    }

    // æ˜¾ç¤ºç¼–è¾‘è´¦å·æ¨¡æ€æ¡†
    function editAccount(id, username, groupLink) {
        currentEditId = id;
        document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = 'ç¼–è¾‘æ¡æ¼è´¦å·';
        document.getElementById('usernameInput').value = username || '';
        document.getElementById('groupLinkInput').value = groupLink || '';
        document.getElementById('accountModal').classList.remove('hidden');
    }
    
    // åˆ é™¤è´¦å·
    async function deleteAccount(id) {
        if (!confirm('ç¡®å®šè¦åˆ é™¤æ­¤æ¡æ¼è´¦å·å—ï¼Ÿåˆ é™¤åæ— æ³•æ¢å¤ï¼')) return;
        
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`/api/fallback-accounts/${id}`, {
                method: 'DELETE',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                },
            });
            
            const data = await response.json();
            if (data.success) {
                showToast('æˆåŠŸ', 'è´¦å·å·²åˆ é™¤');
                loadAccounts();
            } else {
                showToast('é”™è¯¯', data.message || 'åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥', 'error');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥:', error);
            showToast('é”™è¯¯', 'åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥: ' + error.message, 'error');
        }
    }

    // å…³é—­æ¨¡æ€æ¡†
    function closeModal() {
        document.getElementById('accountModal').classList.add('hidden');
    }

    // ä¿å­˜è´¦å·
    async function saveAccount() {
        const username = document.getElementById('usernameInput').value.trim();
        const groupLink = document.getElementById('groupLinkInput').value.trim();

        if (!username && !currentEditId) {
            showToast('é”™è¯¯', 'è¯·è¾“å…¥Telegramç”¨æˆ·å', 'error');
            return;
        }

        try {
            const url = currentEditId 
                ? `/api/fallback-accounts/${currentEditId}`
                : '/api/fallback-accounts';
            
            const method = currentEditId ? 'PUT' : 'POST';
            
            // å¦‚æœæ˜¯ç¼–è¾‘ï¼Œéœ€è¦telegram_id
            let bodyData = {
                username: username || undefined,
                group_link: groupLink
            };
            const response = await fetch(url, {
                method,
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(bodyData),
            });

            const data = await response.json();
            if (data.success) {
                showToast('æˆåŠŸ', currentEditId ? 'æ›´æ–°æˆåŠŸ' : 'æ·»åŠ æˆåŠŸ');
                closeModal();
                loadAccounts();
            } else {
                showToast('é”™è¯¯', data.message || 'æ“ä½œå¤±è´¥', 'error');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥:', error);
            showToast('é”™è¯¯', 'ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥: ' + error.message, 'error');
        }
    }

    // åˆ‡æ¢è´¦å·çŠ¶æ€
    async function toggleAccountStatus(id, isActive) {
        if (!confirm(`ç¡®å®šè¦${isActive ? 'å¯ç”¨' : 'åœç”¨'}æ­¤è´¦å·å—ï¼Ÿ`)) return;

        try {
            const response = await fetch(`/api/fallback-accounts/${id}/status`, {
                method: 'PUT',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    is_active: isActive
                }),
            });

            const data = await response.json();
            if (data.success) {
                showToast('æˆåŠŸ', `è´¦å·å·²${isActive ? 'å¯ç”¨' : 'åœç”¨'}`);
                loadAccounts();
            } else {
                showToast('é”™è¯¯', data.message || 'æ“ä½œå¤±è´¥', 'error');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('æ“ä½œå¤±è´¥:', error);
            showToast('é”™è¯¯', 'æ“ä½œå¤±è´¥: ' + error.message, 'error');
        }
    }

    // æ˜¾ç¤ºæç¤º
    function showToast(title, message, type = 'success') {
        // åˆ›å»ºæç¤ºå…ƒç´ 
        const toast = document.createElement('div');
        toast.className = `fixed top-4 right-4 p-4 rounded-lg shadow-lg z-50 ${
            type === 'success' ? 'bg-green-500' : 'bg-red-500'
        } text-white max-w-xs`;
        
        toast.innerHTML = `
            <div class="font-semibold">${title}</div>
            <div class="text-sm opacity-90">${message}</div>
        `;
        
        document.body.appendChild(toast);
        
        // 3ç§’åè‡ªåŠ¨ç§»é™¤
        setTimeout(() => {
            toast.classList.add('opacity-0', 'transition-opacity', 'duration-300');
            setTimeout(() => {
                document.body.removeChild(toast);
            }, 300);
        }, 3000);
    }

    // é¡µé¢åŠ è½½å®Œæˆåæ‰§è¡Œ
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
        loadAccounts();
    });
</script>

<script>
async function loadBots() {
    try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/bot-configs');
        const data = await response.json();
        const html = data.configs.map(b => `
            <tr class="border-b border-slate-100">
                <td class="px-4 py-3">${b.id}</td>
                <td class="px-4 py-3">${b.bot_username || '-'}</td>
                <td class="px-4 py-3 font-mono text-xs">${b.bot_token.substring(0, 20)}...</td>
                <td class="px-4 py-3">${b.is_active ? '<span class="text-green-600">âœ… å¯ç”¨</span>' : '<span class="text-slate-400">âŒ åœç”¨</span>'}</td>
                <td class="px-4 py-3 text-slate-500">${b.create_time.split(' ')[0]}</td>
                <td class="px-4 py-3 text-right">
                    <button onclick="deleteBot(${b.id})" class="text-red-600 hover:text-red-800">åˆ é™¤</button>
                </td>
            </tr>
        `).join('');
        document.getElementById('botsList').innerHTML = html || '<tr><td colspan="6" class="px-4 py-8 text-center text-slate-400">æš‚æ— æ•°æ®</td></tr>';
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:', error);
    }
}

async function loadAds() {
    try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/advertisements');
        const data = await response.json();
        const html = (data.advertisements || []).map(a => `
            <div class="p-4 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg mb-3">
                <div class="flex items-start justify-between">
                    <div class="flex-1">
                        <h4 class="font-semibold text-slate-900">${a.title}</h4>
                        <p class="text-sm text-slate-600 mt-1">${a.content}</p>
                        <span class="text-xs text-slate-400 mt-2 inline-block">${a.create_time ? a.create_time.split(' ')[0] : ''}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-2 ml-4">
                        <button onclick="publishAd(${a.id})" class="px-3 py-1 bg-green-600 text-white text-xs rounded hover:bg-green-700" title="å‘å¸ƒåˆ°ç¾¤å¹¶ç½®é¡¶">
                            <i class="ti ti-send"></i> å‘å¸ƒ
                        </button>
                        <button onclick="deleteAd(${a.id})" class="text-red-600 hover:text-red-800" title="åˆ é™¤">
                            <i class="ti ti-trash"></i>
                        </button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        `).join('');
        document.getElementById('adsList').innerHTML = html || '<p class="text-slate-400 text-center py-4">æš‚æ— å¹¿å‘Š</p>';
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:', error);
    }
}

function showBotModal() {
    document.getElementById('botModal').classList.remove('hidden');
    document.getElementById('botModal').classList.add('flex');
}

function closeBotModal() {
    document.getElementById('botModal').classList.add('hidden');
}

async function saveBot() {
    const data = {
        bot_token: document.getElementById('botToken').value,
        bot_username: document.getElementById('botUsername').value
    };

    try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/bot-config', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
            body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });

        const result = await response.json();
        if (result.success) {
            showToast('æˆåŠŸ', result.message, 'success');
            closeBotModal();
            loadBots();
        } else {
            showToast('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥', result.message || 'ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥', 'error');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
    }
}

function showAdModal() {
    document.getElementById('adModal').classList.remove('hidden');
    document.getElementById('adModal').classList.add('flex');
}

function closeAdModal() {
    document.getElementById('adModal').classList.add('hidden');
}

async function saveAd() {
    const data = {
        title: document.getElementById('adTitle').value,
        content: document.getElementById('adContent').value
    };

    try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/advertisement', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
            body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });

        const result = await response.json();
        if (result.success) {
            alert(result.message);
            closeAdModal();
            loadAds();
        }
    } catch (error) {
        alert('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥: ' + error.message);
    }
}

async function deleteAd(id) {
    if (!confirm('ç¡®å®šåˆ é™¤æ­¤å¹¿å‘Šå—ï¼Ÿ')) return;
    
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`/api/advertisement/${id}`, {
            method: 'DELETE'
        });
        const result = await response.json();
        if (result.success) {
            alert('åˆ é™¤æˆåŠŸ');
            loadAds();
        } else {
            alert('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥: ' + result.message);
        }
    } catch (error) {
        alert('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥: ' + error.message);
    }
}

async function deleteBot(id) {
    if (!confirm('ç¡®å®šåˆ é™¤æ­¤æœºå™¨äººé…ç½®å—ï¼Ÿ')) return;
    
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`/api/bot-config/${id}`, {
            method: 'DELETE'
        });
        const result = await response.json();
        if (result.success) {
            alert('åˆ é™¤æˆåŠŸ');
            loadBots();
        } else {
            alert('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥: ' + result.message);
        }
    } catch (error) {
        alert('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥: ' + error.message);
    }
}

async function publishAd(id) {
    if (!confirm('ç¡®å®šè¦å°†æ­¤å¹¿å‘Šå‘å¸ƒåˆ°æ‰€æœ‰ä¼šå‘˜ç¾¤å¹¶ç½®é¡¶å—ï¼Ÿ')) return;
    
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`/api/publish-ad/${id}`, {
            method: 'POST'
        });
        const result = await response.json();
        if (result.success) {
            alert(result.message);
        } else {
            alert('å‘å¸ƒå¤±è´¥: ' + result.message);
        }
    } catch (error) {
        alert('å‘å¸ƒå¤±è´¥: ' + error.message);
    }
}

// æ¬¢è¿è¯­ç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°
function showWelcomeModal() {
    document.getElementById('welcomeModal').classList.remove('hidden');
    document.getElementById('welcomeModal').classList.add('flex');
}

function closeWelcomeModal() {
    document.getElementById('welcomeModal').classList.add('hidden');

async function loadWelcomes() {
    try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/welcome-messages');
        const data = await response.json();
        const html = data.messages && data.messages.length > 0 
            ? data.messages.map(w => `
                <div class="p-3 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg mb-2 flex items-start justify-between">
                    <div class="flex-1">
                        <p class="text-sm text-slate-600">${w.content}</p>
                        <span class="text-xs text-slate-400">${w.group_id ? 'ç¾¤:' + w.group_id : 'å…¨å±€'}</span>
                    </div>
                    <button onclick="deleteWelcome(${w.id})" class="text-red-600 hover:text-red-800 ml-2">
                        <i class="ti ti-trash"></i>
                    </button>
                </div>
            `).join('') 
            : '<p class="text-slate-400 text-sm">æš‚æ— æ¬¢è¿è¯­</p>';
        document.getElementById('welcomesList').innerHTML = html;
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('åŠ è½½æ¬¢è¿è¯­å¤±è´¥:', error);
    }
}

async function saveWelcome() {
    const data = {
        group_id: document.getElementById('welcomeGroupId').value || null,
        content: document.getElementById('welcomeContent').value
    };
    
    if (!data.content) {
        alert('è¯·è¾“å…¥æ¬¢è¿è¯­å†…å®¹');
        return;
    }

    try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/welcome-message', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
            body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });
        const result = await response.json();
        if (result.success) {
            alert('ä¿å­˜æˆåŠŸ');
            closeWelcomeModal();
            loadWelcomes();
        } else {
            alert('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥: ' + result.message);
        }
    } catch (error) {
        alert('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥: ' + error.message);
    }
}

async function deleteWelcome(id) {
    if (!confirm('ç¡®å®šåˆ é™¤æ­¤æ¬¢è¿è¯­å—ï¼Ÿ')) return;
    
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`/api/welcome-message/${id}`, {
            method: 'DELETE'
        });
        const result = await response.json();
        if (result.success) {
            alert('åˆ é™¤æˆåŠŸ');
            loadWelcomes();
        } else {
            alert('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥: ' + result.message);
        }
    } catch (error) {
        alert('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥: ' + error.message);
    }
}

// åŠ è½½å¼€å…³çŠ¶æ€
async function loadSwitchSettings() {
    try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/settings');
        const data = await response.json();
        console.log('Settings APIè¿”å›:', data);
        if (data.success && data.settings) {
            const welcomeEnabled = data.settings.welcome_enabled;
            const autoRegisterEnabled = data.settings.auto_register_enabled;
            console.log('welcome_enabled:', welcomeEnabled, 'auto_register_enabled:', autoRegisterEnabled);
            
            // æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦ä¸º'1'æˆ–1æˆ–trueæˆ–'true'
            document.getElementById('welcomeSwitch').checked = welcomeEnabled == '1' || welcomeEnabled == 1 || welcomeEnabled === true;
            document.getElementById('autoRegisterSwitch').checked = autoRegisterEnabled == '1' || autoRegisterEnabled == 1 || autoRegisterEnabled === true;
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('åŠ è½½å¼€å…³è®¾ç½®å¤±è´¥:', error);
    }
}

// ä¿å­˜å¼€å…³çŠ¶æ€
async function saveSwitchSetting(key, value) {
    try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/settings', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
            body: JSON.stringify({ key, value: value ? '1' : '0' })
        });
        const result = await response.json();
        if (!result.success) {
            alert('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥: ' + result.message);
        }
    } catch (error) {
        alert('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥: ' + error.message);
    }
}

// é¡µé¢åŠ è½½
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
    loadBots();
    loadAds();
    loadWelcomes();
    await loadSwitchSettings();
    
    // å¼€å…³äº‹ä»¶ç›‘å¬
    document.getElementById('welcomeSwitch').addEventListener('change', function() {
        console.log('æ¬¢è¿è¯­å¼€å…³å˜æ›´:', this.checked);
        saveSwitchSetting('welcome_enabled', this.checked);
    });
    document.getElementById('autoRegisterSwitch').addEventListener('change', function() {
        console.log('è‡ªåŠ¨æ³¨å†Œå¼€å…³å˜æ›´:', this.checked);
        saveSwitchSetting('auto_register_enabled', this.checked);
    });
});

// Toastæç¤ºå‡½æ•°
function showToast(title, message, type = 'success') {
    // åˆ›å»ºæç¤ºå…ƒç´ 
    const toast = document.createElement('div');
    toast.className = `fixed top-4 right-4 p-4 rounded-lg shadow-lg z-50 ${
        type === 'success' ? 'bg-green-500' : type === 'error' ? 'bg-red-500' : 'bg-blue-500'
    } text-white max-w-xs`;

    toast.innerHTML = `
        <div class="font-semibold">${title}</div>
        <div class="text-sm opacity-90">${message}</div>
    `;

    document.body.appendChild(toast);

    // 3ç§’åè‡ªåŠ¨ç§»é™¤
    setTimeout(() => {
        toast.classList.add('opacity-0', 'transition-opacity', 'duration-300');
        setTimeout(() => {
            if (document.body.contains(toast)) {
                document.body.removeChild(toast);
            }
        }, 300);
    }, 3000);
}
</script>

    <script>
        let currentPage = 1;
        let totalPages = 1;
        let currentMember = null;

        // Toastæç¤º
        function showToast(title, message, type = 'success') {
            const toast = document.getElementById('toast');
            const icon = document.getElementById('toast-icon');
            const titleEl = document.getElementById('toast-title');
            const messageEl = document.getElementById('toast-message');

            const icons = {
                success: '<div class="h-8 w-8 rounded-full bg-green-50 flex items-center justify-center"><i class="ti ti-check text-green-600"></i></div>',
                error: '<div class="h-8 w-8 rounded-full bg-red-50 flex items-center justify-center"><i class="ti ti-alert-triangle text-red-600"></i></div>'
            };

            icon.innerHTML = icons[type] || icons.success;
            titleEl.textContent = title;
            messageEl.textContent = message;

            toast.classList.remove('translate-x-full', 'opacity-0');
            setTimeout(() => {
                toast.classList.add('translate-x-full', 'opacity-0');
            }, 3000);
        }

        // åŠ è½½ç»Ÿè®¡æ•°æ®
        async function loadStatistics() {
            try {
                const response = await fetch('/api/statistics');
                const data = await response.json();

                document.getElementById('totalMembers').textContent = data.total_members.toLocaleString();
                document.getElementById('vipMembers').textContent = data.vip_members.toLocaleString();
                document.getElementById('totalBalance').textContent = data.total_balance.toFixed(2);
                document.getElementById('totalMissed').textContent = data.total_missed.toFixed(2);
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('åŠ è½½ç»Ÿè®¡å¤±è´¥:', error);
                showToast('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        // åŠ è½½ä¼šå‘˜åˆ—è¡¨
        async function loadMembers(page = 1) {
            currentPage = page;
            const search = document.getElementById('searchInput').value;
            
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`/api/members?page=${page}&per_page=20&search=${encodeURIComponent(search)}`);
                const data = await response.json();
                
                displayMembers(data.members);
                displayPagination(data);
                document.getElementById('totalCount').textContent = data.total;
                totalPages = data.pages;
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('åŠ è½½ä¼šå‘˜åˆ—è¡¨å¤±è´¥:', error);
                document.getElementById('membersList').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="9" class="px-6 py-12 text-center text-red-500">åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥ï¼Œè¯·åˆ·æ–°é‡è¯•</td></tr>';
                showToast('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        // æ˜¾ç¤ºä¼šå‘˜åˆ—è¡¨
        function displayMembers(members) {
            if (members.length === 0) {
                document.getElementById('membersList').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="9" class="px-6 py-12 text-center text-slate-400">æš‚æ— æ•°æ®</td></tr>';
                return;
            }

            const html = members.map(m => {
                const vipBadge = m.is_vip 
                    ? '<span class="inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs font-medium bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-700"><i class="ti ti-circle-check"></i> VIP</span>'
                    : '<span class="inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs font-medium bg-slate-100 text-slate-600"><i class="ti ti-user"></i> æ™®é€š</span>';
                
                return `<tr class="hover:bg-slate-50 transition-colors">
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 text-slate-600">${m.id}</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 font-medium text-slate-900">${m.telegram_id}</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 text-indigo-600">@${m.username || 'N/A'}</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 text-slate-600">${m.referrer_name ? '@' + m.referrer_name : '-'}</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 font-bold text-slate-900">${m.balance} U</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 text-rose-500">${m.missed_balance} U</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4">${vipBadge}</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 text-slate-500">${m.register_time ? m.register_time.split(' ')[0] : '-'}</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 text-right space-x-2">
                        <button onclick="viewMember(${m.telegram_id})" class="text-indigo-600 hover:text-indigo-800 font-medium">è¯¦æƒ…</button>
                        <button onclick="editMember(${m.telegram_id})" class="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800 font-medium">ç¼–è¾‘</button>
                        <button onclick="deleteMember(${m.telegram_id}, '@${m.username}')" class="text-red-600 hover:text-red-800 font-medium">åˆ é™¤</button>
                    </td>
                </tr>`;
            }).join('');

            document.getElementById('membersList').innerHTML = html;
        }

        // æ˜¾ç¤ºåˆ†é¡µ
        function displayPagination(data) {
            let html = '';
            
            // ä¸Šä¸€é¡µ
            if (currentPage > 1) {
                html += `<button onclick="loadMembers(${currentPage - 1})" class="px-3 py-1 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-slate-600 hover:bg-slate-50 transition-colors"><i class="ti ti-chevron-left"></i></button>`;
            }
            
            // é¡µç 
            const startPage = Math.max(1, currentPage - 2);
            const endPage = Math.min(data.pages, currentPage + 2);
            
            for (let i = startPage; i <= endPage; i++) {
                if (i === currentPage) {
                    html += `<button class="px-3 py-1 bg-indigo-600 text-white rounded-lg font-medium">${i}</button>`;
                } else {
                    html += `<button onclick="loadMembers(${i})" class="px-3 py-1 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-slate-600 hover:bg-slate-50 transition-colors">${i}</button>`;
                }
            }
            
            // ä¸‹ä¸€é¡µ
            if (currentPage < data.pages) {
                html += `<button onclick="loadMembers(${currentPage + 1})" class="px-3 py-1 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-slate-600 hover:bg-slate-50 transition-colors"><i class="ti ti-chevron-right"></i></button>`;
            }
            
            document.getElementById('pagination').innerHTML = html;
        }

        // æŸ¥çœ‹ä¼šå‘˜è¯¦æƒ…
        async function viewMember(telegramId) {
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`/api/member/${telegramId}`);
                if (!response.ok) {
                    throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}: ${response.statusText}`);
                }
                const member = await response.json();

                // æ£€æŸ¥è¿”å›çš„æ•°æ®æ˜¯å¦æœ‰æ•ˆ
                if (!member || typeof member !== 'object' || !member.telegram_id) {
                    throw new Error('è·å–ä¼šå‘˜ä¿¡æ¯å¤±è´¥ï¼šæ•°æ®æ ¼å¼é”™è¯¯');
                }
                
                const createRow = (label, value) => `
                    <div class="flex justify-between py-3 border-b border-slate-100 last:border-0">
                        <span class="text-sm font-medium text-slate-500">${label}</span>
                        <span class="text-sm text-slate-900 font-medium">${value}</span>
                    </div>`;

                let html = '<div class="bg-slate-50 rounded-lg p-4 space-y-1">';
                html += createRow('ç”¨æˆ·ID', member.telegram_id);
                html += createRow('ç”¨æˆ·å', `@${member.username || 'N/A'}`);
                html += createRow('æ¨èäºº', member.referrer_name ? `@${member.referrer_name}` : 'æ— ');
                html += createRow('ä½™é¢', `<span class="text-emerald-600 font-bold">${member.balance} U</span>`);
                html += createRow('é”™è¿‡ä½™é¢', `<span class="text-rose-500">${member.missed_balance} U</span>`);
                html += createRow('ç¾¤é“¾æ¥', member.group_link || 'æœªè®¾ç½®');
                html += createRow('å¤‡ç”¨å·', member.backup_account || 'æœªè®¾ç½®');
                html += createRow('VIPçŠ¶æ€', member.is_vip ? '<span class="text-emerald-600 font-bold">âœ“ å·²å¼€é€š</span>' : '<span class="text-slate-500">âœ— æœªå¼€é€š</span>');
                html += createRow('æ³¨å†Œæ—¶é—´', member.register_time || '-');
                if (member.vip_upgrade_time) {
                    html += createRow('VIPå¼€é€šæ—¶é—´', member.vip_upgrade_time);
                }
                html += '</div>';

                // æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸‹çº§åˆ—è¡¨
                if (member.downlines && member.downlines.length > 0) {
                    html += '<div class="mt-4"><h4 class="text-sm font-bold text-slate-900 mb-3">ä¸‹çº§ä¼šå‘˜</h4>';
                    html += '<div class="bg-slate-50 rounded-lg p-3 space-y-2 max-h-48 overflow-y-auto">';
                    member.downlines.forEach(d => {
                        const vipIcon = d.is_vip ? '<i class="ti ti-circle-check text-emerald-600"></i>' : '<i class="ti ti-circle-x text-slate-400"></i>';
                        html += `<div class="flex items-center justify-between py-2 px-3 bg-white rounded-lg">
                            <span class="text-sm text-slate-700"><i class="ti ti-user-circle"></i> @${d.username || d.telegram_id}</span>
                            <span>${vipIcon}</span>
                        </div>`;
                    });
                    html += '</div></div>';
                }
                
                document.getElementById('memberDetail').innerHTML = html;
                showModal('detailModal');
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('åŠ è½½è¯¦æƒ…å¤±è´¥:', error);
                showToast('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        // ç¼–è¾‘ä¼šå‘˜
        async function editMember(telegramId) {
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`/api/member/${telegramId}`);
                if (!response.ok) {
                    throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}: ${response.statusText}`);
                }
                currentMember = await response.json();

                // æ£€æŸ¥è¿”å›çš„æ•°æ®æ˜¯å¦æœ‰æ•ˆ
                if (!currentMember || typeof currentMember !== 'object' || !currentMember.telegram_id) {
                    throw new Error('è·å–ä¼šå‘˜ä¿¡æ¯å¤±è´¥ï¼šæ•°æ®æ ¼å¼é”™è¯¯');
                }
                
                const html = `
                    <div class="space-y-4">
                        <div>
                            <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-2">ç”¨æˆ·ID (ä¸å¯ä¿®æ”¹)</label>
                            <input type="text" value="${currentMember.telegram_id}" disabled class="w-full px-3 py-2 bg-slate-100 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-slate-500 cursor-not-allowed">
                        </div>
                        <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                            <div>
                                <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-2">ä½™é¢ (U)</label>
                                <input type="number" step="0.01" id="editBalance" value="${currentMember.balance}" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500">
                            </div>
                            <div>
                                <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-2">é”™è¿‡ä½™é¢ (U)</label>
                                <input type="number" step="0.01" id="editMissedBalance" value="${currentMember.missed_balance}" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500">
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div>
                            <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-2">VIPçŠ¶æ€</label>
                            <select id="editVipStatus" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500">
                                <option value="1" ${currentMember.is_vip ? 'selected' : ''}>VIPä¼šå‘˜</option>
                                <option value="0" ${!currentMember.is_vip ? 'selected' : ''}>æ™®é€šä¼šå‘˜</option>
                            </select>
                        </div>
                        <div>
                            <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-2">ç¾¤é“¾æ¥</label>
                            <input type="text" id="editGroupLink" value="${currentMember.group_link || ''}" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500" placeholder="https://t.me/xxx">
                        </div>
                        <div class="flex gap-3 pt-4 border-t border-slate-200">
                            <button onclick="closeModal('editModal')" class="flex-1 px-4 py-2 border border-slate-200 text-slate-700 rounded-lg hover:bg-slate-50 font-medium transition-colors">å–æ¶ˆ</button>
                            <button onclick="saveEdit()" class="flex-1 px-4 py-2 bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-700 text-white rounded-lg font-medium transition-colors">ä¿å­˜</button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
                
                document.getElementById('editForm').innerHTML = html;
                showModal('editModal');
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('åŠ è½½ç¼–è¾‘è¡¨å•å¤±è´¥:', error);
                showToast('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        // ä¿å­˜ç¼–è¾‘
        async function saveEdit() {
            if (!currentMember) return;
            
            const data = {
                balance: parseFloat(document.getElementById('editBalance').value),
                missed_balance: parseFloat(document.getElementById('editMissedBalance').value),
                is_vip: parseInt(document.getElementById('editVipStatus').value),
                group_link: document.getElementById('editGroupLink').value
            };
            
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`/api/member/${currentMember.telegram_id}`, {
                    method: 'PUT',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify(data)
                });
                
                const result = await response.json();
                if (result.success) {
                    showToast('ä¿å­˜æˆåŠŸ', 'ä¼šå‘˜ä¿¡æ¯å·²æ›´æ–°');
                    closeModal('editModal');
                    loadMembers(currentPage);
                    loadStatistics();
                } else {
                    showToast('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥', result.message, 'error');
                }
            } catch (error) {
                showToast('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        // åˆ é™¤ä¼šå‘˜
        async function deleteMember(telegramId, username) {
            if (!confirm(`ç¡®å®šè¦åˆ é™¤ä¼šå‘˜ ${username} å—ï¼Ÿæ­¤æ“ä½œä¸å¯æ¢å¤ï¼`)) return;
            
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`/api/member/${telegramId}`, { method: 'DELETE' });
                const result = await response.json();
                
                if (result.success) {
                    showToast('åˆ é™¤æˆåŠŸ', 'ä¼šå‘˜å·²åˆ é™¤');
                    loadMembers(currentPage);
                    loadStatistics();
                } else {
                    showToast('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥', result.message, 'error');
                }
            } catch (error) {
                showToast('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        // æœç´¢ä¼šå‘˜
        function searchMembers() {
            loadMembers(1);
        }

        // æ¨¡æ€æ¡†æ§åˆ¶
        function showModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).classList.add('show');
        }

        function closeModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).classList.remove('show');
        }

        // åˆå§‹åŒ–
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            loadStatistics();
            loadMembers();
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
let allMembers = [];
let memberMap = {};

async function loadTree() {
    try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/team-graph-all');
        // å¦‚æœæ²¡æœ‰ä¸“é—¨çš„ all æ¥å£ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ /api/members?per_page=10000 æ¨¡æ‹Ÿ
        // è¿™é‡Œå‡è®¾ä½¿ç”¨çš„æ˜¯ /api/members è·å–æ‰€æœ‰æ•°æ®ï¼Œæˆ–è€…æ‚¨éœ€è¦ç¡®è®¤åç«¯çš„æ¥å£
        let data;
        if (res.ok) {
             data = await res.json();
        } else {
             // Fallback
             const res2 = await fetch('/api/members?per_page=10000');
             data = await res2.json();
        }
        
        if (data.error || !data.members) {
            document.getElementById('treeContainer').innerHTML = 
                '<p class="text-red-500 text-center py-8">åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥: æ•°æ®æ ¼å¼é”™è¯¯</p>';
            return;
        }
        
        allMembers = data.members;
        
        // æ„å»ºæ˜ å°„ (æ·»åŠ æ•°æ®éªŒè¯)
        memberMap = {};
        allMembers.forEach(m => {
            if (m && m.telegram_id) {
                memberMap[m.telegram_id] = m;
            }
        });
        
        // æ‰¾å‡ºé¡¶çº§ç”¨æˆ· (æ²¡æœ‰æ¨èäººï¼Œæˆ–æ¨èäººä¸åœ¨ç°æœ‰åˆ—è¡¨ä¸­)
        const topMembers = allMembers.filter(m => {
            return !m.referrer_id || !memberMap[m.referrer_id];
        });
        
        // æ›´æ–°ç»Ÿè®¡ (ç®€å•è®¡ç®—)
        document.getElementById('stat-total').textContent = allMembers.length;
        document.getElementById('stat-top').textContent = topMembers.length;
        document.getElementById('stat-vip').textContent = allMembers.filter(m => m.is_vip).length;
        // æ·±åº¦è®¡ç®—ç•¥ç¹çï¼Œè¿™é‡Œæš‚ç•¥

        const html = topMembers.map(m => renderNode(m, 0)).join('');
        document.getElementById('treeContainer').innerHTML = html || '<p class="text-slate-400 text-center py-8">æš‚æ— æ•°æ®</p>';
            
    } catch (error) {
        console.error(error);
        document.getElementById('treeContainer').innerHTML = 
            '<p class="text-red-500 text-center py-8">åŠ è½½é”™è¯¯: ' + error.message + '</p>';
    }
}

function renderNode(member, depth) {
    if (!member) return '';

    // å®‰å…¨è·å–å±æ€§
    const username = member.username || 'æ— å';
    const tgId = member.telegram_id || 'IDæœªçŸ¥';
    const isVip = member.is_vip;

    // å®‰å…¨è¿‡æ»¤å­èŠ‚ç‚¹ (ç¡®ä¿må’Œmemberéƒ½æœ‰æœ‰æ•ˆçš„telegram_id)
    const children = allMembers.filter(m =>
        m && m.referrer_id && member.telegram_id && m.referrer_id === member.telegram_id
    );
    const hasChildren = children.length > 0;
    const isTopLevel = depth === 0;
    
    let html = `
        <div class="tree-item" data-id="${tgId}">
            <div class="tree-toggle flex items-center gap-2 py-1 px-2 rounded-lg ${hasChildren ? '' : 'pl-6'}">
                ${hasChildren ? `
                    <span class="toggle-icon text-slate-400 w-4 text-center" onclick="toggleNode(${tgId})">
                        <i class="ti ti-chevron-right text-sm"></i>
                    </span>
                ` : ''}
                <div class="member-card ${isTopLevel ? 'top-level' : ''}">
                    <span class="text-lg">${isVip ? 'ğŸ‘‘' : 'ğŸ‘¤'}</span>
                    <div>
                        <span class="px-2 py-0.5 text-xs rounded bg-green-100 text-green-700 font-bold mr-2">ç¬¬${depth + 1}å±‚</span>
                        <span class="font-medium text-slate-900">@${username}</span>
                        <span class="text-xs text-slate-400 ml-2">${tgId}</span>
                    </div>
                    ${member.is_vip ? '<span class="vip-badge">VIP</span>' : ''}
                    <span class="text-xs text-slate-500">
                        ç›´æ¨: ${member.direct_count || 0}
                    </span>
                    <a href="/team-graph/${member.telegram_id}" class="text-xs text-indigo-600 hover:text-indigo-800 ml-2">
                        <i class="ti ti-external-link"></i>
                    </a>
                </div>
            </div>
            ${hasChildren ? `
                <div class="tree-children tree-node" id="children-${member.telegram_id}">
                    ${children.map(c => renderNode(c, depth + 1)).join('')}
                </div>
            ` : ''}
        </div>
    `;
    return html;
}

function toggleNode(id) {
    const children = document.getElementById('children-' + id);
    const icon = document.querySelector(`[data-id="${id}"] .toggle-icon i`);
    
    if (children) {
        children.classList.toggle('expanded');
        if (icon) {
            icon.classList.toggle('ti-chevron-right');
            icon.classList.toggle('ti-chevron-down');
        }
    }
}

function expandAll() {
    document.querySelectorAll('.tree-children').forEach(el => {
        el.classList.add('expanded');
    });
    document.querySelectorAll('.toggle-icon i').forEach(el => {
        el.classList.remove('ti-chevron-right');
        el.classList.add('ti-chevron-down');
    });
}

function collapseAll() {
    document.querySelectorAll('.tree-children').forEach(el => {
        el.classList.remove('expanded');
    });
    document.querySelectorAll('.toggle-icon i').forEach(el => {
        el.classList.add('ti-chevron-right');
        el.classList.remove('ti-chevron-down');
    });
}

function searchMember() {
    const query = document.getElementById('searchInput').value.toLowerCase().trim();
    
    // ç§»é™¤æ‰€æœ‰é«˜äº®
    document.querySelectorAll('.member-card').forEach(el => {
        el.classList.remove('highlighted');
    });
    
    if (!query) return;
    
    // æœç´¢åŒ¹é…
    allMembers.forEach(m => {
        if (!m) return; // è·³è¿‡æ— æ•ˆæˆå‘˜
        const username = m.username || '';
        const telegramId = m.telegram_id || '';
        if (username.toLowerCase().includes(query) ||
            telegramId.toString().includes(query)) {
            // é«˜äº®å¹¶å±•å¼€åˆ°è¯¥èŠ‚ç‚¹
            const item = document.querySelector(`[data-id="${m.telegram_id}"]`);
            if (item) {
                item.querySelector('.member-card').classList.add('highlighted');
                
                // å±•å¼€çˆ¶çº§
                let parent = item.parentElement;
                while (parent) {
                    if (parent.classList.contains('tree-children')) {
                        parent.classList.add('expanded');
                        const icon = parent.previousElementSibling?.querySelector('.toggle-icon i');
                        if (icon) {
                            icon.classList.remove('ti-chevron-right');
                            icon.classList.add('ti-chevron-down');
                        }
                    }
                    parent = parent.parentElement;
                }
                
                // æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°è§†å›¾
                item.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
            }
        }
    });
}

document.getElementById('searchInput').addEventListener('keypress', function(e) {
    if (e.key === 'Enter') searchMember();
});

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', loadTree);
</script>
{% endblock %}

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // è‡ªåŠ¨é«˜äº®å½“å‰é¡µé¢å¯¼èˆªæ 
            const currentPath = window.location.pathname;
            const navLinks = document.querySelectorAll('nav a[href]');
            navLinks.forEach(link => {
                const href = link.getAttribute('href');
                // ç§»é™¤æ‰€æœ‰é«˜äº®
                link.classList.remove('bg-indigo-50', 'text-indigo-600', 'border', 'border-indigo-100/50', 'shadow-sm');
                link.classList.add('hover:bg-slate-50', 'text-slate-500', 'hover:text-slate-900');
                
                // é«˜äº®å½“å‰é¡µé¢
                if ((currentPath === '/' && href === '/') || (currentPath === href && href !== '/')) {
                    link.classList.remove('hover:bg-slate-50', 'text-slate-500', 'hover:text-slate-900');
                    link.classList.add('bg-indigo-50', 'text-indigo-600', 'border', 'border-indigo-100/50', 'shadow-sm');
                }
            });
        });

let currentServiceId = null;

        function showToast(title, message, type = 'success') {
            const toast = document.getElementById('toast');
            const icon = document.getElementById('toast-icon');
            document.getElementById('toast-title').textContent = title;
            document.getElementById('toast-message').textContent = message;
            icon.innerHTML = type === 'success' 
                ? '<div class="h-8 w-8 rounded-full bg-green-50 flex items-center justify-center"><i class="ti ti-check text-green-600"></i></div>'
                : '<div class="h-8 w-8 rounded-full bg-red-50 flex items-center justify-center"><i class="ti ti-alert-triangle text-red-600"></i></div>';
            toast.classList.remove('translate-x-full', 'opacity-0');
            setTimeout(() => toast.classList.add('translate-x-full', 'opacity-0'), 3000);
        }

        async function loadServices() {
            try {
                const res = await fetch('/api/customer_services');
                const services = await res.json();
                
                const tbody = document.getElementById('servicesList');
                if (!services || services.length === 0) {
                    tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="px-6 py-12 text-center text-slate-400">æš‚æ— å®¢æœ</td></tr>';
                    return;
                }

                tbody.innerHTML = services.map(s => `
                    <tr class="hover:bg-slate-50">
                        <td class="px-6 py-4">${s.id}</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4 font-medium">${s.name}</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4 text-indigo-600">${s.link}</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4 text-right space-x-2">
                            <button onclick="editService(${s.id})" class="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800 font-medium">ç¼–è¾‘</button>
                            <button onclick="deleteService(${s.id}, '${s.name}')" class="text-red-600 hover:text-red-800 font-medium">åˆ é™¤</button>
                        </td>
                    </tr>
                `).join('');
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:', error);
                document.getElementById('servicesList').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="px-6 py-12 text-center text-red-500">åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥</td></tr>';
                showToast('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        function showAddModal() {
            currentServiceId = null;
            document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = 'æ·»åŠ å®¢æœ';
            document.getElementById('serviceName').value = '';
            document.getElementById('serviceLink').value = '';
            document.getElementById('editModal').classList.add('show');
        }

        async function editService(id) {
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`/api/customer_services/${id}`);
                const s = await res.json();
                
                currentServiceId = id;
                document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = 'ç¼–è¾‘å®¢æœ';
                document.getElementById('serviceName').value = s.name;
                document.getElementById('serviceLink').value = s.link;
                document.getElementById('editModal').classList.add('show');
            } catch (error) {
                showToast('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        async function saveService() {
            const name = document.getElementById('serviceName').value.trim();
            const link = document.getElementById('serviceLink').value.trim();

            if (!name || !link) {
                showToast('éªŒè¯å¤±è´¥', 'è¯·å¡«å†™æ‰€æœ‰å¿…å¡«é¡¹', 'error');
                return;
            }

            try {
                const res = await fetch(currentServiceId ? `/api/customer_services/${currentServiceId}` : '/api/customer_services', {
                    method: currentServiceId ? 'PUT' : 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ name, link })
                });
                
                const result = await res.json();
                if (result.success) {
                    showToast('ä¿å­˜æˆåŠŸ', currentServiceId ? 'å®¢æœå·²æ›´æ–°' : 'å®¢æœå·²æ·»åŠ ');
                    closeModal();
                    loadServices();
                } else {
                    showToast('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥', result.message, 'error');
                }
            } catch (error) {
                showToast('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        async function deleteService(id, name) {
            if (!confirm(`ç¡®å®šåˆ é™¤å®¢æœ"${name}"å—ï¼Ÿ`)) return;
            
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`/api/customer_services/${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' });
                const result = await res.json();
                
                if (result.success) {
                    showToast('åˆ é™¤æˆåŠŸ', 'å®¢æœå·²åˆ é™¤');
                    loadServices();
                } else {
                    showToast('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥', result.message, 'error');
                }
            } catch (error) {
                showToast('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        function closeModal() {
            document.getElementById('editModal').classList.remove('show');
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', loadServices);
</script>
{% endblock %}

<script>
(function() {
    let page = 1, search = '', pages = 1, startDate = '', endDate = '';

    async function loadStats() {
        try {
            let url = '/api/recharges/stats';
            const params = [];
            if (startDate) params.push(`start_date=${encodeURIComponent(startDate)}`);
            if (endDate) params.push(`end_date=${encodeURIComponent(endDate)}`);
            if (params.length > 0) url += '?' + params.join('&');

            const res = await fetch(url);
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success && data.stats) {
                const stats = data.stats;
                document.getElementById('total-amount').textContent = stats.total_amount.toFixed(2) + ' U';
                document.getElementById('success-amount').textContent = stats.success_amount.toFixed(2) + ' U';
                document.getElementById('failed-amount').textContent = stats.failed_amount.toFixed(2) + ' U';
                document.getElementById('total-count').textContent = stats.total_count + ' ç¬”';
                document.getElementById('success-count').textContent = stats.success_count + ' ç¬”';
                document.getElementById('failed-count').textContent = stats.failed_count + ' ç¬”';
                document.getElementById('pending-count').textContent = stats.pending_count + ' ç¬”';
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('Load stats error:', e);
        }
    }

    async function load() {
        let url = `/api/recharges?page=${page}`;
        if (search) url += `&search=${encodeURIComponent(search)}`;
        if (startDate) url += `&start_date=${encodeURIComponent(startDate)}`;
        if (endDate) url += `&end_date=${encodeURIComponent(endDate)}`;

        try {
            const res = await fetch(url);
            const data = await res.json();
            console.log('API response:', data);
            
            const tbody = document.getElementById('table-body');
            const empty = document.getElementById('empty');
            
            // APIè¿”å›çš„æ˜¯recordså­—æ®µ
            const records = data.records || [];
            
            if (records.length === 0) {
                tbody.innerHTML = '';
                empty.classList.remove('hidden');
            } else {
                empty.classList.add('hidden');
                tbody.innerHTML = records.map(item => {
                    let statusHtml = '';
                    if (item.status === 'pending') {
                        statusHtml = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs bg-amber-50 text-amber-700">å¾…æ”¯ä»˜</span>';
                    } else if (item.status === 'completed' || item.status === 'success') {
                        statusHtml = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-700">å·²å®Œæˆ</span>';
                    } else {
                        statusHtml = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs bg-slate-100 text-slate-600">' + (item.status || 'æœªçŸ¥') + '</span>';
                    }
                    const canSetPaid = (item.status === 'pending' || item.status === 'created' || !item.status);
                    const actionHtml = canSetPaid
                        ? `<button class="ml-2 px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs bg-indigo-500 text-white hover:bg-indigo-600" onclick="markRechargePaid(${item.id})">è®¾ä¸ºå·²æ”¯ä»˜</button>`
                        : '';
                    return `<tr class="hover:bg-slate-50">
                        <td class="px-6 py-4 text-slate-500">#${item.id}</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4">
                            <div class="font-medium text-slate-900">@${item.username || 'N/A'}</div>
                            <div class="text-xs text-slate-500">ID: ${item.telegram_id}</div>
                        </td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4">
                            <span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs ${item.type === 'å¼€é€šVIP' ? 'bg-purple-50 text-purple-700' : 'bg-blue-50 text-blue-700'}">${item.type}</span>
                        </td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4 font-bold text-slate-700">${item.amount} U</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4 text-slate-500 text-xs">${item.order_number || '-'}</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4 text-slate-500 text-xs">${item.create_time || '-'}</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4">
                            <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
                                ${statusHtml}
                                ${actionHtml}
                            </div>
                        </td>
                    </tr>`;
                }).join('');
            }
            
            document.getElementById('total').textContent = data.total || 0;
            document.getElementById('page-num').textContent = data.page || 1;
            const perPage = data.per_page || 20;
            pages = Math.ceil((data.total || 0) / perPage) || 1;
            document.getElementById('prev-btn').disabled = page <= 1;
            document.getElementById('next-btn').disabled = page >= pages;

            // åŠ è½½ç»Ÿè®¡æ•°æ®
            await loadStats();
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('Load error:', e);
        }
    }
    
    document.getElementById('search-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {
        search = document.getElementById('search-input').value.trim();
        page = 1;
        load();
    });
    
    document.getElementById('search-input').addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
        if (e.key === 'Enter') {
            search = document.getElementById('search-input').value.trim();
            page = 1;
            load();
        }
    });
    
    document.getElementById('prev-btn').addEventListener('click', () => { if (page > 1) { page--; load(); } });
    document.getElementById('next-btn').addEventListener('click', () => { if (page < pages) { page++; load(); } });

    // æ—¥æœŸç­›é€‰åŠŸèƒ½
    document.getElementById('date-filter-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {
        startDate = document.getElementById('start-date').value;
        endDate = document.getElementById('end-date').value;

        // éªŒè¯æ—¥æœŸèŒƒå›´
        if (startDate && endDate && startDate > endDate) {
            alert('å¼€å§‹æ—¥æœŸä¸èƒ½æ™šäºç»“æŸæ—¥æœŸ');
            return;
        }

        page = 1; // é‡ç½®åˆ°ç¬¬ä¸€é¡µ
        loadStats(); // é‡æ–°åŠ è½½ç»Ÿè®¡æ•°æ®
        load(); // é‡æ–°åŠ è½½å……å€¼è®°å½•åˆ—è¡¨
    });

    // ä»Šæ—¥ç­›é€‰
    document.getElementById('today-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {
        const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
        startDate = today;
        endDate = today;
        document.getElementById('start-date').value = today;
        document.getElementById('end-date').value = today;

        page = 1; // é‡ç½®åˆ°ç¬¬ä¸€é¡µ
        loadStats(); // é‡æ–°åŠ è½½ç»Ÿè®¡æ•°æ®
        load(); // é‡æ–°åŠ è½½å……å€¼è®°å½•åˆ—è¡¨
    });

    // æ˜¨æ—¥ç­›é€‰
    document.getElementById('yesterday-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {
        const yesterday = new Date();
        yesterday.setDate(yesterday.getDate() - 1);
        const yesterdayStr = yesterday.toISOString().split('T')[0];
        startDate = yesterdayStr;
        endDate = yesterdayStr;
        document.getElementById('start-date').value = yesterdayStr;
        document.getElementById('end-date').value = yesterdayStr;

        page = 1; // é‡ç½®åˆ°ç¬¬ä¸€é¡µ
        loadStats(); // é‡æ–°åŠ è½½ç»Ÿè®¡æ•°æ®
        load(); // é‡æ–°åŠ è½½å……å€¼è®°å½•åˆ—è¡¨
    });

    document.getElementById('clear-date-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {
        startDate = '';
        endDate = '';
        document.getElementById('start-date').value = '';
        document.getElementById('end-date').value = '';

        page = 1; // é‡ç½®åˆ°ç¬¬ä¸€é¡µ
        loadStats(); // é‡æ–°åŠ è½½ç»Ÿè®¡æ•°æ®
        load(); // é‡æ–°åŠ è½½å……å€¼è®°å½•åˆ—è¡¨
    });

    // åˆå§‹åŒ–åŠ è½½
    loadStats(); // å…ˆåŠ è½½ç»Ÿè®¡æ•°æ®
    load(); // å†åŠ è½½åˆ—è¡¨æ•°æ®
})();

async function markRechargePaid(id) {
    if (!confirm('ç¡®å®šå°†è¯¥è®¢å•æ ‡è®°ä¸ºã€å·²æ”¯ä»˜ã€‘å¹¶ä¸ºç”¨æˆ·å¢åŠ ä½™é¢å—ï¼Ÿ')) return;
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`/api/recharges/${id}/status`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ status: 'completed' })
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (data.success) {
            showRechargeTip(data.message || 'å·²æ›´æ–°ä¸ºå·²æ”¯ä»˜', 'success');
            const evt = new Event('click');
            document.getElementById('search-btn').dispatchEvent(evt);
        } else {
            showRechargeTip(data.message || 'æ“ä½œå¤±è´¥', 'error');
        }
    } catch (e) {
        showRechargeTip('è¯·æ±‚å¤±è´¥ï¼š' + e.message, 'error');
    }
}

function showRechargeTip(msg, type='info') {
    const el = document.getElementById('recharge-tip');
    el.textContent = msg;
    el.classList.remove('hidden');
    el.classList.remove('bg-emerald-50','text-emerald-700','bg-red-50','text-red-700','bg-slate-100','text-slate-700');
    if (type === 'success') {
        el.classList.add('bg-emerald-50','text-emerald-700');
    } else if (type === 'error') {
        el.classList.add('bg-red-50','text-red-700');
    } else {
        el.classList.add('bg-slate-100','text-slate-700');
    }
    setTimeout(() => { el.classList.add('hidden'); }, 2500);
}
</script>
{% endblock %}

    <script>
        const loginForm = document.getElementById('loginForm');
        const errorMessage = document.getElementById('errorMessage');
        const errorText = document.getElementById('errorText');
        const loginBtn = document.getElementById('loginBtn');
        const btnText = document.getElementById('btnText');
        const btnIcon = document.getElementById('btnIcon');
        const btnSpinner = document.getElementById('btnSpinner');

        loginForm.addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
            e.preventDefault();
            
            // ç®€å•çš„åŠ è½½çŠ¶æ€
            loginBtn.disabled = true;
            loginBtn.classList.add('opacity-75', 'cursor-not-allowed');
            btnText.textContent = 'ç™»å½•ä¸­...';
            btnIcon.classList.add('hidden');
            btnSpinner.classList.remove('hidden');
            errorMessage.classList.add('hidden');

            const formData = new FormData(loginForm);
            const data = Object.fromEntries(formData.entries());
            // å¤„ç† checkbox
            data.remember = document.getElementById('remember').checked;

            try {
                const response = await fetch('/login', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify(data)
                });

                const result = await response.json();

                if (result.success) {
                    window.location.href = '/';
                } else {
                    throw new Error(result.message || 'ç™»å½•å¤±è´¥');
                }
            } catch (error) {
                errorText.textContent = error.message;
                errorMessage.classList.remove('hidden');
                
                // æ¢å¤æŒ‰é’®çŠ¶æ€
                loginBtn.disabled = false;
                loginBtn.classList.remove('opacity-75', 'cursor-not-allowed');
                btnText.textContent = 'ç™» å½•';
                btnIcon.classList.remove('hidden');
                btnSpinner.classList.add('hidden');
                
                // éœ‡åŠ¨æ•ˆæœ
                const card = document.querySelector('.max-w-md');
                card.classList.add('animate-pulse');
                setTimeout(() => card.classList.remove('animate-pulse'), 200);
            }
        });
    </script>

<script>
// åŠ è½½ç»Ÿè®¡æ•°æ®
async function loadDashboardStats() {
    try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/dashboard/stats');
        const data = await response.json();
        
        if (data.success) {
            const stats = data.data;
            
            // æ›´æ–°æ ¸å¿ƒæ•°æ®
            document.getElementById('total-members').textContent = stats.total_members || 0;
            document.getElementById('vip-members').textContent = stats.vip_members || 0;
            document.getElementById('today-register').textContent = stats.today_register || 0;
            document.getElementById('today-vip').textContent = stats.today_vip || 0;
            
            // æ›´æ–°æ”¶ç›Šæ•°æ®
            document.getElementById('today-income').textContent = (stats.today_income || 0) + ' U';
            document.getElementById('yesterday-income').textContent = (stats.yesterday_income || 0) + ' U';
            document.getElementById('month-income').textContent = (stats.month_income || 0) + ' U';
            document.getElementById('total-income').textContent = (stats.total_income || 0) + ' U';
            
            // æ›´æ–°è¶‹åŠ¿æ•°æ®
            document.getElementById('yesterday-register').textContent = stats.yesterday_register || 0;
            document.getElementById('yesterday-vip').textContent = stats.yesterday_vip || 0;
            document.getElementById('month-register').textContent = stats.month_register || 0;
            document.getElementById('month-vip').textContent = stats.month_vip || 0;
            
            // åŠ è½½æ¡æ¼è´¦å·æ’è¡Œ
            loadFallbackAccounts(stats.fallback_accounts || []);
            
            // ç»˜åˆ¶è¶‹åŠ¿å›¾
            drawTrendChart(stats.trend_data || {});
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('åŠ è½½ç»Ÿè®¡æ•°æ®å¤±è´¥:', error);
    }
}

// åŠ è½½æ¡æ¼è´¦å·æ’è¡Œ
function loadFallbackAccounts(accounts) {
    const tbody = document.getElementById('fallback-accounts-table');
    tbody.innerHTML = '';
    
    accounts.forEach((account, index) => {
        const tr = document.createElement('tr');
        tr.className = 'border-b border-slate-100 hover:bg-slate-50';
        
        const rankClass = index === 0 ? 'text-yellow-500' : index === 1 ? 'text-slate-400' : index === 2 ? 'text-orange-400' : 'text-slate-600';
        
        tr.innerHTML = `
            <td class="px-4 py-3">
                <span class="font-bold ${rankClass}">
                    ${index === 0 ? 'ğŸ¥‡' : index === 1 ? 'ğŸ¥ˆ' : index === 2 ? 'ğŸ¥‰' : '#' + (index + 1)}
                </span>
            </td>
            <td class="px-4 py-3 font-medium text-slate-800">${account.username || 'æœªçŸ¥'}</td>
            <td class="px-4 py-3 text-slate-600">${account.telegram_id || '-'}</td>
            <td class="px-4 py-3 font-semibold text-green-600">${account.balance || 0} U</td>
            <td class="px-4 py-3 font-semibold text-blue-600">${account.total_earned || 0} U</td>
            <td class="px-4 py-3">
                <span class="px-2 py-1 bg-green-100 text-green-700 rounded text-xs">
                    ${account.is_vip ? 'VIP' : 'æ™®é€š'}
                </span>
            </td>
        `;
        tbody.appendChild(tr);
    });
}

// ç»˜åˆ¶è¶‹åŠ¿å›¾è¡¨
let trendChart = null;
function drawTrendChart(trendData) {
    const ctx = document.getElementById('trend-chart');
    
    if (trendChart) {
        trendChart.destroy();
    }
    
    trendChart = new Chart(ctx, {
        type: 'line',
        data: {
            labels: trendData.labels || [],
            datasets: [
                {
                    label: 'æ³¨å†Œäººæ•°',
                    data: trendData.register_counts || [],
                    borderColor: 'rgb(59, 130, 246)',
                    backgroundColor: 'rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.1)',
                    tension: 0.4,
                    fill: true
                },
                {
                    label: 'å¼€é€šVIP',
                    data: trendData.vip_counts || [],
                    borderColor: 'rgb(168, 85, 247)',
                    backgroundColor: 'rgba(168, 85, 247, 0.1)',
                    tension: 0.4,
                    fill: true
                }
            ]
        },
        options: {
            responsive: true,
            maintainAspectRatio: true,
            plugins: {
                legend: {
                    display: true,
                    position: 'top'
                }
            },
            scales: {
                y: {
                    beginAtZero: true,
                    ticks: {
                        stepSize: 1
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    });
}

// é¡µé¢åŠ è½½æ—¶æ‰§è¡Œ

    loadDashboardStats();
    
    // æ¯30ç§’åˆ·æ–°ä¸€æ¬¡æ•°æ®
    setInterval(loadDashboardStats, 30000);
});
