<script>
let selectedGroups = new Set();
let allGroups = [];
let broadcastTargets = [];

function showToast(title, message, type = 'success') {
    const toast = document.getElementById('toast');
    document.getElementById('toast-title').textContent = title;
    document.getElementById('toast-message').textContent = message;
    document.getElementById('toast-icon').innerHTML = type === 'success'
        ? '<div class="h-7 w-7 rounded-full bg-green-50 flex items-center justify-center"><i class="ti ti-check text-green-600"></i></div>'
        : '<div class="h-7 w-7 rounded-full bg-red-50 flex items-center justify-center"><i class="ti ti-alert-triangle text-red-600"></i></div>';
    toast.classList.remove('translate-x-full', 'opacity-0');
    setTimeout(() => toast.classList.add('translate-x-full', 'opacity-0'), 3000);
}

async function loadGroups() {
    const search = document.getElementById('searchInput').value;
    try {
        selectedGroups.clear(); // æ¸…ç©ºé€‰ä¸­çŠ¶æ€
        document.getElementById('checkAll').checked = false;
        const res = await fetch(`/api/member-groups?search=${encodeURIComponent(search)}`);
        const data = await res.json();
        allGroups = data.groups || [];
        displayGroups(allGroups);
        document.getElementById('totalCount').textContent = allGroups.length;
        document.getElementById('showCount').textContent = allGroups.length;
    } catch (error) {
        document.getElementById('groupsBody').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="10" class="px-4 py-8 text-center text-red-500">åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥</td></tr>';
    }
}

function displayGroups(groups) {
    const tbody = document.getElementById('groupsBody');
    
    if (!groups || groups.length === 0) {
        tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="10" class="px-4 py-8 text-center text-slate-400">æš‚æ— æ•°æ®ï¼Œç‚¹å‡»"æ·»åŠ "æŒ‰é’®åˆ›å»ºç¾¤ç»„</td></tr>';
        return;
    }
    
    tbody.innerHTML = groups.map(g => `
        <tr class="hover:bg-slate-50">
            <td class="px-2 py-2 text-center"><input type="checkbox" class="group-check w-4 h-4 rounded" data-id="${g.id}" onchange="toggleSelect(${g.id})"></td>
            <td class="px-2 py-2 text-slate-500">${g.id}</td>
            <td class="px-2 py-2 font-mono">${g.telegram_id || '-'}</td>
            <td class="px-2 py-2 font-medium text-indigo-600">${g.group_name || 'æœªè®¾ç½®'}</td>
            <td class="px-2 py-2">${g.owner_username ? '@' + g.owner_username : '-'}</td>
            <td class="px-2 py-2 text-center"><span class="px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-xs ${g.group_type === 'channel' ? 'bg-purple-100 text-purple-700' : 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-700'}">${g.group_type === 'channel' ? 'é¢‘é“' : 'ç¾¤ç»„'}</span></td>
            <td class="px-2 py-2 text-center">
                <label class="relative inline-flex items-center cursor-pointer">
                    <input type="checkbox" ${g.schedule_broadcast ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="toggleSchedule(${g.id}, this.checked)" class="sr-only peer">
                    <div class="w-9 h-5 bg-slate-200 peer-focus:outline-none rounded-full peer peer-checked:after:translate-x-full peer-checked:after:border-white after:content-[''] after:absolute after:top-[2px] after:left-[2px] after:bg-white after:rounded-full after:h-4 after:w-4 after:transition-all peer-checked:bg-green-500"></div>
                </label>
            </td>
            <td class="px-2 py-2 text-slate-500">${g.create_time || '-'}</td>
            <td class="px-2 py-2 text-center">${g.is_bot_admin ? '<span class="text-green-600 font-bold">æ˜¯</span>' : '<span class="text-red-500">å¦</span>'}</td>
            <td class="px-2 py-2">
                <div class="flex items-center justify-center gap-1">
                    <button onclick="verifyGroup(${g.id})" class="px-2 py-1 text-xs rounded bg-cyan-500 hover:bg-cyan-600 text-white font-medium">éªŒè¯</button>
                    <button onclick="editGroup(${g.id})" class="px-2 py-1 text-xs rounded bg-blue-500 hover:bg-blue-600 text-white font-medium">ç¼–è¾‘</button>
                    <button onclick="deleteGroup(${g.id})" class="px-2 py-1 text-xs rounded bg-red-500 hover:bg-red-600 text-white font-medium">åˆ é™¤</button>
                </div>
            </td>
        </tr>
    `).join('');
}

function toggleAll() {
    const checked = document.getElementById('checkAll').checked;
    document.querySelectorAll('.group-check').forEach(cb => {
        cb.checked = checked;
        const id = parseInt(cb.dataset.id);
        if (checked) selectedGroups.add(id);
        else selectedGroups.delete(id);
    });
}

function toggleSelect(id) {
    const cb = document.querySelector(`.group-check[data-id="${id}"]`);
    if (cb && cb.checked) {
        selectedGroups.add(id);
    } else {
        selectedGroups.delete(id);
    }
    console.log('Selected groups:', [...selectedGroups]);
}

async function toggleSchedule(id, enabled) {
    try {
        await fetch(`/api/member-groups/${id}`, {
            method: 'PUT',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ schedule_broadcast: enabled ? 1 : 0 })
        });
        showToast('æˆåŠŸ', enabled ? 'å·²å¼€å¯å®šæ—¶ç¾¤å‘' : 'å·²å…³é—­å®šæ—¶ç¾¤å‘');
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('å¤±è´¥', 'æ“ä½œå¤±è´¥', 'error');
    }
}

function showAddModal() {
    document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = 'æ·»åŠ ç¾¤ç»„';
    document.getElementById('editId').value = '';
    document.getElementById('addTelegramId').value = '';
    document.getElementById('addGroupId').value = '';
    document.getElementById('addGroupName').value = '';
    document.getElementById('addGroupLink').value = '';
    document.getElementById('addOwnerUsername').value = '';
    document.getElementById('addGroupType').value = 'group';
    document.getElementById('addIsBotAdmin').value = '1';
    document.getElementById('addScheduleBroadcast').value = '1';
    showModal('addModal');
}

function editGroup(id) {
    const g = allGroups.find(x => x.id === id);
    if (!g) return;
    
    document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = 'ç¼–è¾‘ç¾¤ç»„';
    document.getElementById('editId').value = g.id;
    document.getElementById('addTelegramId').value = g.telegram_id || '';
    document.getElementById('addGroupId').value = g.group_id || '';
    document.getElementById('addGroupName').value = g.group_name || '';
    document.getElementById('addGroupLink').value = g.group_link || '';
    document.getElementById('addOwnerUsername').value = g.owner_username || '';
    document.getElementById('addGroupType').value = g.group_type || 'group';
    document.getElementById('addIsBotAdmin').value = g.is_bot_admin ? '1' : '0';
    document.getElementById('addScheduleBroadcast').value = g.schedule_broadcast ? '1' : '0';
    showModal('addModal');
}

async function saveGroup() {
    const editId = document.getElementById('editId').value;
    const data = {
        telegram_id: document.getElementById('addTelegramId').value || null,
        group_id: document.getElementById('addGroupId').value || null,
        group_name: document.getElementById('addGroupName').value,
        group_link: document.getElementById('addGroupLink').value,
        owner_username: document.getElementById('addOwnerUsername').value,
        group_type: document.getElementById('addGroupType').value,
        is_bot_admin: parseInt(document.getElementById('addIsBotAdmin').value),
        schedule_broadcast: parseInt(document.getElementById('addScheduleBroadcast').value)
    };
    
    try {
        const url = editId ? `/api/member-groups/${editId}` : '/api/member-groups';
        const method = editId ? 'PUT' : 'POST';
        const res = await fetch(url, {
            method: method,
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });
        const result = await res.json();
        if (result.success) {
            showToast('æˆåŠŸ', editId ? 'ç¾¤ç»„å·²æ›´æ–°' : 'ç¾¤ç»„å·²æ·»åŠ ');
            closeModal('addModal');
            loadGroups();
        } else {
            showToast('å¤±è´¥', result.message || 'æ“ä½œå¤±è´¥', 'error');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('é”™è¯¯', error.message, 'error');
    }
}

async function deleteGroup(id) {
    if (!confirm('ç¡®å®šè¦åˆ é™¤è¿™ä¸ªç¾¤ç»„å—ï¼Ÿ')) return;
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`/api/member-groups/${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' });
        const result = await res.json();
        if (result.success) {
            showToast('æˆåŠŸ', 'ç¾¤ç»„å·²åˆ é™¤');
            loadGroups();
        }
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('å¤±è´¥', 'åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥', 'error');
    }
}

function editSelected() {
    if (selectedGroups.size !== 1) {
        showToast('æç¤º', 'è¯·é€‰æ‹©ä¸€ä¸ªç¾¤ç»„è¿›è¡Œç¼–è¾‘', 'error');
        return;
    }
    editGroup([...selectedGroups][0]);
}

async function deleteSelected() {
    if (selectedGroups.size === 0) {
        showToast('æç¤º', 'è¯·å…ˆé€‰æ‹©è¦åˆ é™¤çš„ç¾¤ç»„', 'error');
        return;
    }
    if (!confirm(`ç¡®å®šè¦åˆ é™¤é€‰ä¸­çš„ ${selectedGroups.size} ä¸ªç¾¤ç»„å—ï¼Ÿ`)) return;
    
    for (const id of selectedGroups) {
        await fetch(`/api/member-groups/${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' });
    }
    showToast('æˆåŠŸ', `å·²åˆ é™¤ ${selectedGroups.size} ä¸ªç¾¤ç»„`);
    selectedGroups.clear();
    loadGroups();
}

function refreshAll() {
    loadGroups();
    showToast('æˆåŠŸ', 'å·²åˆ·æ–°');
}

async function verifyGroup(id) {
    showToast('éªŒè¯ä¸­', 'æ­£åœ¨éªŒè¯ç¾¤ç»„çŠ¶æ€...');
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`/api/member-groups/${id}/verify`, { method: 'POST' });
        const result = await res.json();
        if (result.success) {
            showToast('æˆåŠŸ', result.message || 'éªŒè¯æˆåŠŸ');
            loadGroups();
        } else {
            showToast('å¤±è´¥', result.message || 'éªŒè¯å¤±è´¥', 'error');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('é”™è¯¯', 'éªŒè¯è¯·æ±‚å¤±è´¥', 'error');
    }
}

function broadcastSelected() {
    if (selectedGroups.size === 0) {
        showToast('æç¤º', 'è¯·å…ˆé€‰æ‹©è¦ç¾¤å‘çš„ç¾¤ç»„', 'error');
        return;
    }
    broadcastTargets = [...selectedGroups];
    document.getElementById('broadcastInfo').textContent = `å°†å‘ ${broadcastTargets.length} ä¸ªé€‰ä¸­çš„ç¾¤ç»„å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯`;
    document.getElementById('broadcastMessage').value = '';
    showModal('broadcastModal');
}

function broadcastAll() {
    if (allGroups.length === 0) {
        showToast('æç¤º', 'æš‚æ— ç¾¤ç»„å¯ç¾¤å‘', 'error');
        return;
    }
    broadcastTargets = allGroups.map(g => g.id);
    document.getElementById('broadcastInfo').textContent = `å°†å‘å…¨éƒ¨ ${broadcastTargets.length} ä¸ªç¾¤ç»„å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯`;
    document.getElementById('broadcastMessage').value = '';
    showModal('broadcastModal');
}

async function sendBroadcast() {
    const message = document.getElementById('broadcastMessage').value.trim();
    if (!message) {
        showToast('æç¤º', 'è¯·è¾“å…¥æ¶ˆæ¯å†…å®¹', 'error');
        return;
    }
    
    try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/member-groups/broadcast', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ group_ids: broadcastTargets, message: message })
        });
        const result = await res.json();
        if (result.success) {
            showToast('æç¤º', `å·²æäº¤ç¾¤å‘ä»»åŠ¡ï¼Œå°†å‘é€åˆ° ${result.sent_count || 0} ä¸ªç¾¤ç»„ï¼ˆå®é™…å‘é€ç”±åå°æœºå™¨äººæ‰§è¡Œï¼‰`);
            closeModal('broadcastModal');
        } else {
            showToast('å¤±è´¥', result.message || 'å‘é€å¤±è´¥', 'error');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('é”™è¯¯', error.message, 'error');
    }
}

// --------- æ–°å¢ï¼šé€‰æ‹©å¹¶åˆ†é…/å‘é€ç¾¤å‘å†…å®¹é€»è¾‘ ----------
let modalTargetGroups = []; // è¦æ“ä½œçš„ç¾¤ç»„id
let broadcastMessagesCache = [];

function openSelectBroadcastModal(targetGroupIds) {
    modalTargetGroups = targetGroupIds || [];
    document.getElementById('selectBroadcastInfo').textContent = `å°†å¯¹ ${modalTargetGroups.length} ä¸ªç¾¤è¿›è¡Œæ“ä½œ`;
    document.getElementById('broadcastList').innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-slate-400 py-6" id="broadcastLoading">åŠ è½½ä¸­...</div>';
    showModal('selectBroadcastModal');
    loadBroadcastMessagesForModal();
}

async function loadBroadcastMessagesForModal() {
    try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/broadcast/messages');
        const data = await res.json();
        const msgs = data.messages || [];
        broadcastMessagesCache = msgs;

        if (!msgs.length) {
            document.getElementById('broadcastList').innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-slate-400 py-6">æš‚æ— ç¾¤å‘å†…å®¹</div>';
            return;
        }

        const html = msgs.map(m => {
            return `<div class="p-2 border rounded flex items-start gap-3">
                <div class="w-6"><input type="checkbox" class="select-broadcast-checkbox" data-id="${m.id}"></div>
                <div class="flex-1">
                    <div class="font-medium">${m.title || 'æœªå‘½å'}</div>
                    <div class="text-xs text-slate-600">${(m.content || '').substring(0,200)}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="text-xs text-slate-500">é—´éš”: ${m.broadcast_interval || 120} åˆ†é’Ÿ</div>
            </div>`;
        }).join('');
        document.getElementById('broadcastList').innerHTML = html;
    } catch (error) {
        document.getElementById('broadcastList').innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-red-500 py-6">åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥</div>';
    }
}

function broadcastSelected() {
    if (selectedGroups.size === 0) {
        showToast('æç¤º', 'è¯·å…ˆé€‰æ‹©è¦ç¾¤å‘çš„ç¾¤ç»„', 'error');
        return;
    }
    openSelectBroadcastModal([...selectedGroups]);
}

function broadcastAll() {
    if (allGroups.length === 0) {
        showToast('æç¤º', 'æš‚æ— ç¾¤ç»„å¯ç¾¤å‘', 'error');
        return;
    }
    openSelectBroadcastModal(allGroups.map(g => g.id));
}

async function assignSelectedBroadcasts() {
    const checkboxes = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.select-broadcast-checkbox')).filter(cb => cb.checked);
    if (checkboxes.length === 0) {
        showToast('æç¤º', 'è¯·é€‰æ‹©è¦åˆ†é…çš„ç¾¤å‘å†…å®¹', 'error');
        return;
    }
    if (modalTargetGroups.length === 0) {
        showToast('æç¤º', 'æ²¡æœ‰ç›®æ ‡ç¾¤ç»„', 'error');
        return;
    }

    try {
        // å¯¹æ¯ä¸ªç¾¤ç»„å’Œæ¯ä¸ªæ¶ˆæ¯å‘èµ· assignment è¯·æ±‚
        for (const gid of modalTargetGroups) {
            for (const cb of checkboxes) {
                const mid = parseInt(cb.dataset.id);
                await fetch(`/api/member-groups/${gid}/broadcasts`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ message_id: mid, is_active: 1 })
                });
            }
        }
        showToast('æˆåŠŸ', `å·²å°† ${checkboxes.length} æ¡å†…å®¹åˆ†é…åˆ° ${modalTargetGroups.length} ä¸ªç¾¤`);
        closeModal('selectBroadcastModal');
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('å¤±è´¥', 'åˆ†é…å¤±è´¥', 'error');
    }
}

async function sendSelectedBroadcasts() {
    const checkboxes = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.select-broadcast-checkbox')).filter(cb => cb.checked);
    if (checkboxes.length === 0) {
        showToast('æç¤º', 'è¯·é€‰æ‹©è¦å‘é€çš„ç¾¤å‘å†…å®¹', 'error');
        return;
    }
    if (modalTargetGroups.length === 0) {
        showToast('æç¤º', 'æ²¡æœ‰ç›®æ ‡ç¾¤ç»„', 'error');
        return;
    }

    const message_ids = checkboxes.map(cb => parseInt(cb.dataset.id));
    try {
        for (const gid of modalTargetGroups) {
            await fetch(`/api/member-groups/${gid}/broadcast/send`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ message_ids: message_ids })
            });
        }
        showToast('æˆåŠŸ', `å·²æäº¤å‘é€ä»»åŠ¡ç»™ ${modalTargetGroups.length} ä¸ªç¾¤`);
        closeModal('selectBroadcastModal');
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('å¤±è´¥', 'å‘é€å¤±è´¥', 'error');
    }
}


function showModal(id) { document.getElementById(id).classList.add('show'); }
function closeModal(id) { document.getElementById(id).classList.remove('show'); }

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', loadGroups);

<script>
// æ ¼å¼åŒ–æ•°å­—
        function formatNumber(num) {
            return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US').format(num);
        }

        // æ ¼å¼åŒ–é‡‘é¢
        function formatMoney(num) {
            return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', { style: 'decimal', minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 }).format(num);
        }

        // åŠ è½½ç»Ÿè®¡æ•°æ®
        async function loadStats() {
            try {
                // åŠ è½½åŸºç¡€ç»Ÿè®¡
                const statsRes = await fetch('/api/statistics');
                const stats = await statsRes.json();
                
                document.getElementById('stat-total-members').textContent = formatNumber(stats.total_members);
                document.getElementById('stat-vip-members').textContent = formatNumber(stats.vip_members);
                document.getElementById('stat-total-balance').textContent = formatMoney(stats.total_balance);
                document.getElementById('stat-missed-balance').textContent = formatMoney(stats.total_missed);
                
                if (stats.total_members > 0) {
                    const ratio = ((stats.vip_members / stats.total_members) * 100).toFixed(1);
                    document.getElementById('vip-ratio-badge').textContent = `${ratio}%`;
                }

                // åŠ è½½å›¾è¡¨æ•°æ®
                const chartRes = await fetch('/api/statistics/chart');
                const chartData = await chartRes.json();

                // æ¸²æŸ“å¢é•¿è¶‹åŠ¿å›¾
                const ctxGrowth = document.getElementById('growthChart').getContext('2d');
                new Chart(ctxGrowth, {
                    type: 'line',
                    data: {
                        labels: chartData.growth.labels,
                        datasets: [{
                            label: 'æ–°å¢ç”¨æˆ·',
                            data: chartData.growth.data,
                            borderColor: '#4f46e5',
                            backgroundColor: 'rgba(79, 70, 229, 0.1)',
                            borderWidth: 2,
                            tension: 0.4,
                            fill: true,
                            pointBackgroundColor: '#ffffff',
                            pointBorderColor: '#4f46e5',
                            pointBorderWidth: 2,
                            pointRadius: 4,
                            pointHoverRadius: 6
                        }]
                    },
                    options: {
                        responsive: true,
                        maintainAspectRatio: false,
                        plugins: {
                            legend: {
                                display: false
                            }
                        },
                        scales: {
                            y: {
                                beginAtZero: true,
                                grid: {
                                    borderDash: [2, 4],
                                    color: '#e2e8f0',
                                    drawBorder: false,
                                },
                                ticks: {
                                    stepSize: 1
                                }
                            },
                            x: {
                                grid: {
                                    display: false
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });

                // æ¸²æŸ“æ„æˆå›¾
                const ctxComp = document.getElementById('compositionChart').getContext('2d');
                new Chart(ctxComp, {
                    type: 'doughnut',
                    data: {
                        labels: ['VIPç”¨æˆ·', 'æ™®é€šç”¨æˆ·'],
                        datasets: [{
                            data: [chartData.composition.vip, chartData.composition.normal],
                            backgroundColor: [
                                '#4f46e5', // Indigo 600
                                '#e2e8f0'  // Slate 200
                            ],
                            borderWidth: 0,
                            hoverOffset: 4
                        }]
                    },
                    options: {
                        responsive: true,
                        maintainAspectRatio: false,
                        cutout: '75%',
                        plugins: {
                            legend: {
                                position: 'bottom',
                                labels: {
                                    usePointStyle: true,
                                    padding: 20,
                                    font: {
                                        size: 12
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });

                // æ›´æ–°æ–‡å­—æ•°æ®
                document.getElementById('chart-vip-count').textContent = formatNumber(chartData.composition.vip);
                document.getElementById('chart-normal-count').textContent = formatNumber(chartData.composition.normal);

            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error loading stats:', error);
            }
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            loadStats();
            
            // è‡ªåŠ¨é«˜äº®å½“å‰é¡µé¢å¯¼èˆªæ 
            const currentPath = window.location.pathname;
            const navLinks = document.querySelectorAll('nav a[href]');
            navLinks.forEach(link => {
                const href = link.getAttribute('href');
                // ç§»é™¤æ‰€æœ‰é«˜äº®
                link.classList.remove('bg-indigo-50', 'text-indigo-600', 'border', 'border-indigo-100/50', 'shadow-sm');
                link.classList.add('hover:bg-slate-50', 'text-slate-500', 'hover:text-slate-900');
                
                // é«˜äº®å½“å‰é¡µé¢
                if ((currentPath === '/' && href === '/') || (currentPath === href && href !== '/')) {
                    link.classList.remove('hover:bg-slate-50', 'text-slate-500', 'hover:text-slate-900');
                    link.classList.add('bg-indigo-50', 'text-indigo-600', 'border', 'border-indigo-100/50', 'shadow-sm');
                }
            });
        });
</script>

<script>
let currentCategoryId = null;
let currentResourceId = null;

function showToast(title, message, type = 'success') {
    const toast = document.getElementById('toast');
    const icon = document.getElementById('toast-icon');
    document.getElementById('toast-title').textContent = title;
    document.getElementById('toast-message').textContent = message;
    icon.innerHTML = type === 'success' 
        ? '<div class="h-8 w-8 rounded-full bg-green-50 flex items-center justify-center"><i class="ti ti-check text-green-600"></i></div>'
        : '<div class="h-8 w-8 rounded-full bg-red-50 flex items-center justify-center"><i class="ti ti-alert-triangle text-red-600"></i></div>';
    toast.classList.remove('translate-x-full', 'opacity-0');
    setTimeout(() => toast.classList.add('translate-x-full', 'opacity-0'), 3000);
}

function switchTab(tab) {
    document.getElementById('tab-categories').className = tab === 'categories' 
        ? 'pb-3 px-1 border-b-2 border-indigo-600 text-indigo-600 font-medium text-sm' 
        : 'pb-3 px-1 border-b-2 border-transparent text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-700 font-medium text-sm';
    document.getElementById('tab-resources').className = tab === 'resources' 
        ? 'pb-3 px-1 border-b-2 border-indigo-600 text-indigo-600 font-medium text-sm' 
        : 'pb-3 px-1 border-b-2 border-transparent text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-700 font-medium text-sm';
    document.getElementById('content-categories').style.display = tab === 'categories' ? 'block' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('content-resources').style.display = tab === 'resources' ? 'block' : 'none';
    if (tab === 'resources') loadResources();
}

async function loadCategories() {
    try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/resource_categories');
        const data = await res.json();
        const tbody = document.getElementById('categoriesList');
        tbody.innerHTML = !data.categories || data.categories.length === 0 
            ? '<tr><td colspan="3" class="px-6 py-12 text-center text-slate-400">æš‚æ— åˆ†ç±»</td></tr>'
            : data.categories.map(c => `
                <tr class="hover:bg-slate-50">
                    <td class="px-6 py-4">${c.id}</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 font-medium">${c.name}</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 text-right space-x-2">
                        <button onclick="editCategory(${c.id})" class="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800 font-medium">ç¼–è¾‘</button>
                        <button onclick="deleteCategory(${c.id},'${c.name}')" class="text-red-600 hover:text-red-800 font-medium">åˆ é™¤</button>
                    </td>
                </tr>
            `).join('');
        
        // æ›´æ–°åˆ†ç±»é€‰æ‹©å™¨
        const selects = [document.getElementById('filterCategory'), document.getElementById('resourceCategory')];
        selects.forEach(select => {
            if (!select) return;
            const current = select.value;
            select.innerHTML = select.id === 'filterCategory' ? '<option value="">å…¨éƒ¨åˆ†ç±»</option>' : '<option value="">è¯·é€‰æ‹©åˆ†ç±»</option>';
            if (data.categories) {
                data.categories.forEach(c => select.innerHTML += `<option value="${c.id}">${c.name}</option>`);
            }
            select.value = current;
        });
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
    }
}

async function loadResources() {
    const filterEl = document.getElementById('filterCategory');
    const categoryId = filterEl ? filterEl.value : '';
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`/api/resources${categoryId ? '?category_id=' + categoryId : ''}`);
        const data = await res.json();
        const tbody = document.getElementById('resourcesList');
        tbody.innerHTML = !data.resources || data.resources.length === 0
            ? '<tr><td colspan="7" class="px-6 py-12 text-center text-slate-400">æš‚æ— èµ„æº</td></tr>'
            : data.resources.map(r => `
                <tr class="hover:bg-slate-50">
                    <td class="px-6 py-4">${r.id}</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4">${r.category_name || '-'}</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 font-medium">${r.name}</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 text-indigo-600 text-xs">${r.link}</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4"><span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs ${r.type === 'group' ? 'bg-blue-50 text-blue-700' : 'bg-purple-50 text-purple-700'}">${r.type === 'group' ? 'ç¾¤ç»„' : 'é¢‘é“'}</span></td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 font-semibold">${(r.member_count / 1000).toFixed(1)}K</td>
                    <td class="px-6 py-4 text-right space-x-2">
                        <button onclick="editResource(${r.id})" class="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800 font-medium">ç¼–è¾‘</button>
                        <button onclick="deleteResource(${r.id},'${r.name}')" class="text-red-600 hover:text-red-800 font-medium">åˆ é™¤</button>
                    </td>
                </tr>
            `).join('');
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
    }
}

function showAddCategoryModal() {
    currentCategoryId = null;
    document.getElementById('categoryModalTitle').textContent = 'æ·»åŠ åˆ†ç±»';
    document.getElementById('categoryName').value = '';
    document.getElementById('categoryModal').classList.add('show');
}

async function editCategory(id) {
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`/api/resource_categories/${id}`);
        const cat = await res.json();
        currentCategoryId = id;
        document.getElementById('categoryModalTitle').textContent = 'ç¼–è¾‘åˆ†ç±»';
        document.getElementById('categoryName').value = cat.name;
        document.getElementById('categoryModal').classList.add('show');
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
    }
}

async function saveCategory() {
    const name = document.getElementById('categoryName').value.trim();
    if (!name) return showToast('éªŒè¯å¤±è´¥', 'è¯·è¾“å…¥åˆ†ç±»åç§°', 'error');
    
    try {
        const res = await fetch(currentCategoryId ? `/api/resource_categories/${currentCategoryId}` : '/api/resource_categories', {
            method: currentCategoryId ? 'PUT' : 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ name, parent_id: 0 })
        });
        const result = await res.json();
        if (result.success) {
            showToast('ä¿å­˜æˆåŠŸ', currentCategoryId ? 'åˆ†ç±»å·²æ›´æ–°' : 'åˆ†ç±»å·²æ·»åŠ ');
            closeCategoryModal();
            loadCategories();
        } else {
            showToast('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥', result.message || 'æœªçŸ¥é”™è¯¯', 'error');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
    }
}

async function deleteCategory(id, name) {
    if (!confirm(`ç¡®å®šåˆ é™¤åˆ†ç±»"${name}"å—ï¼Ÿ`)) return;
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`/api/resource_categories/${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' });
        const result = await res.json();
        if (result.success) {
            showToast('åˆ é™¤æˆåŠŸ', 'åˆ†ç±»å·²åˆ é™¤');
            loadCategories();
        } else {
            showToast('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥', result.message || 'æœªçŸ¥é”™è¯¯', 'error');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
    }
}

function closeCategoryModal() {
    document.getElementById('categoryModal').classList.remove('show');
}

function showAddResourceModal() {
    currentResourceId = null;
    document.getElementById('resourceModalTitle').textContent = 'æ·»åŠ èµ„æº';
    document.getElementById('resourceName').value = '';
    document.getElementById('resourceLink').value = '';
    document.getElementById('resourceType').value = 'group';
    document.getElementById('resourceCount').value = '';
    document.getElementById('resourceCategory').value = '';
    document.getElementById('resourceModal').classList.add('show');
}

async function editResource(id) {
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`/api/resources/${id}`);
        const r = await res.json();
        currentResourceId = id;
        document.getElementById('resourceModalTitle').textContent = 'ç¼–è¾‘èµ„æº';
        document.getElementById('resourceCategory').value = r.category_id || '';
        document.getElementById('resourceName').value = r.name || '';
        document.getElementById('resourceLink').value = r.link || '';
        document.getElementById('resourceType').value = r.type || 'group';
        document.getElementById('resourceCount').value = r.member_count || '';
        document.getElementById('resourceModal').classList.add('show');
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
    }
}

async function saveResource() {
    const data = {
        category_id: parseInt(document.getElementById('resourceCategory').value) || 0,
        name: document.getElementById('resourceName').value.trim(),
        link: document.getElementById('resourceLink').value.trim(),
        type: document.getElementById('resourceType').value,
        member_count: parseInt(document.getElementById('resourceCount').value) || 0
    };
    
    if (!data.name || !data.link) {
        return showToast('éªŒè¯å¤±è´¥', 'è¯·å¡«å†™èµ„æºåç§°å’Œé“¾æ¥', 'error');
    }
    
    try {
        const res = await fetch(currentResourceId ? `/api/resources/${currentResourceId}` : '/api/resources', {
            method: currentResourceId ? 'PUT' : 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });
        const result = await res.json();
        if (result.success) {
            showToast('ä¿å­˜æˆåŠŸ', currentResourceId ? 'èµ„æºå·²æ›´æ–°' : 'èµ„æºå·²æ·»åŠ ');
            closeResourceModal();
            loadResources();
        } else {
            showToast('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥', result.message || 'æœªçŸ¥é”™è¯¯', 'error');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
    }
}

async function deleteResource(id, name) {
    if (!confirm(`ç¡®å®šåˆ é™¤èµ„æº"${name}"å—ï¼Ÿ`)) return;
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`/api/resources/${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' });
        const result = await res.json();
        if (result.success) {
            showToast('åˆ é™¤æˆåŠŸ', 'èµ„æºå·²åˆ é™¤');
            loadResources();
        } else {
            showToast('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥', result.message || 'æœªçŸ¥é”™è¯¯', 'error');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
    }
}

function closeResourceModal() {
    document.getElementById('resourceModal').classList.remove('show');
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', loadCategories);
</script>

<script>
let currentPage = 1;
let currentMember = null;
let selectedMembers = new Set();
let memberBroadcastMode = 'selected';

function showToast(title, message, type = 'success') {
    const toast = document.getElementById('toast');
    document.getElementById('toast-title').textContent = title;
    document.getElementById('toast-message').textContent = message;
    document.getElementById('toast-icon').innerHTML = type === 'success'
        ? '<div class="h-7 w-7 rounded-full bg-green-50 flex items-center justify-center"><i class="ti ti-check text-green-600"></i></div>'
        : '<div class="h-7 w-7 rounded-full bg-red-50 flex items-center justify-center"><i class="ti ti-alert-triangle text-red-600"></i></div>';
    toast.classList.remove('translate-x-full', 'opacity-0');
    setTimeout(() => toast.classList.add('translate-x-full', 'opacity-0'), 3000);
}

async function loadStatistics() {
    try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/statistics');
        const data = await response.json();
        console.log('Graph API Response:', data);
        console.log('downlines:', data.downlines);
        document.getElementById('totalMembers').textContent = data.total_members.toLocaleString();
        document.getElementById('vipMembers').textContent = data.vip_members.toLocaleString();
        document.getElementById('totalBalance').textContent = data.total_balance.toFixed(2);
        document.getElementById('totalMissed').textContent = data.total_missed.toFixed(2);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('åŠ è½½ç»Ÿè®¡å¤±è´¥:', error);
    }
}

async function loadMembers(page = currentPage) {
    currentPage = page;
    const search = document.getElementById('searchInput').value;
    const filterType = document.getElementById('filterType').value;
    const perPage = document.getElementById('perPage').value;
    
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`/api/members?page=${page}&per_page=${perPage}&search=${encodeURIComponent(search)}&filter=${filterType}`);
        const data = await response.json();
        console.log('Graph API Response:', data);
        console.log('downlines:', data.downlines);
        displayMembers(data.members);
        displayPagination(data);
        document.getElementById('totalCount').textContent = data.total;
        document.getElementById('currentPageNum').textContent = currentPage;
        document.getElementById('totalPageNum').textContent = data.pages || 1;
        selectedMembers.clear();
        document.getElementById('checkAll').checked = false;
    } catch (error) {
        document.getElementById('membersList').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="14" class="px-4 py-8 text-center text-red-500">åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥</td></tr>';
    }
}

function displayMembers(members) {
    if (!members || members.length === 0) {
        document.getElementById('membersList').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="14" class="px-4 py-8 text-center text-slate-400">æš‚æ— æ•°æ®</td></tr>';
        return;
    }
    
    const yesNo = (v) => v ? '<span class="text-green-600 font-bold">æ˜¯</span>' : '<span class="text-slate-400">å¦</span>';
    
    const html = members.map(m => `<tr class="hover:bg-slate-50 border-b border-slate-100">
        <td class="py-1 text-center" style="padding-left:4px;padding-right:4px;"><input type="checkbox" class="member-check w-3 h-3 rounded" data-id="${m.telegram_id}" onchange="toggleSelect(${m.telegram_id})"></td>
        <td class="py-1 text-slate-500" style="padding-left:4px;padding-right:4px;">${m.id}</td>
        <td class="py-1 font-mono text-slate-700" style="padding-left:4px;padding-right:4px;">${m.telegram_id}</td>
        <td class="py-1" style="padding-left:4px;padding-right:0px;">
            <div class="text-sm font-semibold ${m.is_fallback ? 'text-orange-600' : 'text-indigo-600'}">@${m.username || 'N/A'}</div>
            ${
                m.backup_account
                    ? '<div class="text-[11px] text-slate-500">å¤‡:' + (m.backup_account.startsWith('@') ? m.backup_account : '@' + m.backup_account) + '</div>'
                    : '<div class="text-[11px] text-slate-400">å¤‡: â€”</div>'
            }
        </td>
        <td class="py-1 text-slate-500" style="padding-left:2px;padding-right:4px;">
            <div class="text-[11px] leading-tight text-slate-600">æ¨èäººID: ${m.referrer_id || 'â€”'}</div>
            <div class="text-[11px] leading-tight text-indigo-600 font-medium">${m.referrer_username ? '@' + m.referrer_username : 'â€”'}</div>
        </td>
        <td class="py-1 text-left" style="padding-left:4px;padding-right:4px;">
            <div class="text-sm font-semibold text-emerald-600">å‰©ä½™: ${m.balance} U</div>
            <div class="text-xs text-rose-500">é”™è¿‡: ${m.missed_balance || 0} U</div>
        </td>
        <td class="py-1 text-left" style="padding-left:4px;padding-right:4px;">
            ${m.group_link ? `<div class="flex items-center gap-1">
                <span class="text-blue-600 break-all">${m.group_link}</span>
                <button class="px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[11px] border border-slate-200 rounded hover:bg-slate-100" onclick="copyText('${m.group_link}')">å¤åˆ¶</button>
            </div>` : '<span class="text-slate-400">æœªè®¾ç½®</span>'}
        </td>
        <td class="py-1 text-center" style="padding-left:4px;padding-right:4px;">
            <div class="border border-slate-200 rounded px-1.5 py-1 text-[11px] leading-tight space-y-1">
                <div class="flex justify-between"><span>æ‹‰ç¾¤</span><span>${yesNo(m.is_group_bound)}</span></div>
                <div class="border-t border-slate-100 pt-1 flex justify-between"><span>ç¾¤ç®¡</span><span>${yesNo(m.is_bot_admin)}</span></div>
                <div class="border-t border-slate-100 pt-1 flex justify-between"><span>åŠ ç¾¤</span><span>${yesNo(m.is_joined_upline)}</span></div>
            </div>
        </td>
        <td class="py-1 text-center" style="padding-left:4px;padding-right:4px;">
            ${m.is_vip ? `<span class="px-1 py-0.5 rounded font-semibold ${m.is_fallback ? 'bg-orange-200 text-orange-800' : 'bg-amber-100 text-amber-700'}">VIP</span>` : '<span class="text-slate-400">æ™®é€š</span>'}
        </td>
        <td class="py-1 text-center text-slate-600 text-xs" style="padding-left:4px;padding-right:4px;">
            <div>ç›´æ¨: ${m.direct_count || 0}</div>
            <div>å›¢é˜Ÿ: ${m.team_count || 0}</div>
        </td>
        <td class="py-1 text-left text-[11px] text-slate-600" style="padding-left:4px;padding-right:4px;">
            <div>æ³¨å†Œ: ${m.register_time ? m.register_time.replace('T', ' ') : 'â€”'}</div>
            <div>VIP: ${m.vip_time ? m.vip_time.replace('T', ' ') : 'â€”'}</div>
        </td>
        <td class="py-1" style="padding-left:4px;padding-right:4px;"><div class="flex items-center gap-1"><button onclick="showGraph(${m.telegram_id})" class="px-2 py-0.5 text-xs rounded bg-purple-500 text-white">å›¾è°±</button><button onclick="editMember(${m.telegram_id})" class="px-2 py-0.5 text-xs rounded bg-blue-500 text-white">ç¼–è¾‘</button><button onclick="deleteMember(${m.telegram_id}, '@${m.username}')" class="px-2 py-0.5 text-xs rounded bg-red-500 text-white">åˆ é™¤</button></div></td>
    </tr>`).join('');
    document.getElementById('membersList').innerHTML = html;
}

async function copyText(text) {
    try {
        if (navigator.clipboard && navigator.clipboard.writeText) {
            await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
        } else {
            const ta = document.createElement('textarea');
            ta.value = text;
            document.body.appendChild(ta);
            ta.select();
            document.execCommand('copy');
            document.body.removeChild(ta);
        }
        showToast('å·²å¤åˆ¶', text, 'success');
    } catch (e) {
        showToast('å¤åˆ¶å¤±è´¥', e.message || 'è¯·æ‰‹åŠ¨å¤åˆ¶', 'error');
    }
}

function displayPagination(data) {
    let html = '';
    const totalPages = data.pages || 1;
    
    html += `<button onclick="loadMembers(${currentPage-1})" ${currentPage <= 1 ? 'disabled' : ''} class="px-2 py-1 text-sm border rounded hover:bg-slate-50 disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed"><i class="ti ti-chevron-left"></i></button>`;
    
    let startPage = Math.max(1, currentPage - 2);
    let endPage = Math.min(totalPages, currentPage + 2);
    
    if (startPage > 1) {
        html += `<button onclick="loadMembers(1)" class="px-2 py-1 text-sm border rounded hover:bg-slate-50">1</button>`;
        if (startPage > 2) html += `<span class="px-1 text-slate-400">...</span>`;
    }
    
    for (let i = startPage; i <= endPage; i++) {
        html += i === currentPage
            ? `<button class="px-2 py-1 text-sm bg-indigo-600 text-white rounded">${i}</button>`
            : `<button onclick="loadMembers(${i})" class="px-2 py-1 text-sm border rounded hover:bg-slate-50">${i}</button>`;
    }
    
    if (endPage < totalPages) {
        if (endPage < totalPages - 1) html += `<span class="px-1 text-slate-400">...</span>`;
        html += `<button onclick="loadMembers(${totalPages})" class="px-2 py-1 text-sm border rounded hover:bg-slate-50">${totalPages}</button>`;
    }
    
    html += `<button onclick="loadMembers(${currentPage+1})" ${currentPage >= totalPages ? 'disabled' : ''} class="px-2 py-1 text-sm border rounded hover:bg-slate-50 disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed"><i class="ti ti-chevron-right"></i></button>`;
    
    document.getElementById('pagination').innerHTML = html;
}

function toggleAll() {
    const checked = document.getElementById('checkAll').checked;
    document.querySelectorAll('.member-check').forEach(cb => {
        cb.checked = checked;
        const id = parseInt(cb.dataset.id);
        if (checked) selectedMembers.add(id);
        else selectedMembers.delete(id);
    });
}

function toggleSelect(id) {
    if (selectedMembers.has(id)) selectedMembers.delete(id);
    else selectedMembers.add(id);
}

function selectAll() {
    document.getElementById('checkAll').checked = true;
    toggleAll();
}

function showMemberBroadcastModal(mode) {
    memberBroadcastMode = mode;
    if (mode === 'selected' && selectedMembers.size === 0) {
        showToast('æç¤º', 'è¯·å…ˆé€‰æ‹©è¦ç¾¤å‘çš„ä¼šå‘˜', 'error');
        return;
    }
    const scopeText = mode === 'all'
        ? 'å°†å‘å½“å‰æ‰€æœ‰ä¼šå‘˜å‘é€ä¸‹é¢è¿™æ¡æ¶ˆæ¯ã€‚'
        : `å°†å‘å·²å‹¾é€‰çš„ ${selectedMembers.size} ä½ä¼šå‘˜å‘é€ä¸‹é¢è¿™æ¡æ¶ˆæ¯ã€‚`;
    document.getElementById('memberBroadcastScope').textContent = scopeText;
    document.getElementById('memberBroadcastMessage').value = '';
    showModal('memberBroadcastModal');
}

async function sendMemberBroadcast() {
    const message = document.getElementById('memberBroadcastMessage').value.trim();
    if (!message) {
        showToast('é”™è¯¯', 'è¯·è¾“å…¥è¦å‘é€çš„æ¶ˆæ¯å†…å®¹', 'error');
        return;
    }

    const payload = {
        message: message,
        all: memberBroadcastMode === 'all',
        member_ids: memberBroadcastMode === 'selected' ? Array.from(selectedMembers) : []
    };

    try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/members/broadcast', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify(payload)
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (data.success) {
            showToast('ç¾¤å‘å·²æäº¤', data.message || `å·²åŠ å…¥å‘é€é˜Ÿåˆ—ï¼Œé¢„è®¡å‘ ${data.count || 0} ä½ä¼šå‘˜å‘é€`);
            closeModal('memberBroadcastModal');
        } else {
            showToast('ç¾¤å‘å¤±è´¥', data.message || 'æäº¤ç¾¤å‘ä»»åŠ¡å¤±è´¥', 'error');
        }
    } catch (e) {
        showToast('ç¾¤å‘å¤±è´¥', e.message, 'error');
    }
}

async function batchDelete() {
    if (selectedMembers.size === 0) {
        showToast('æç¤º', 'è¯·å…ˆé€‰æ‹©è¦åˆ é™¤çš„ä¼šå‘˜', 'error');
        return;
    }
    if (!confirm(`ç¡®å®šè¦åˆ é™¤é€‰ä¸­çš„ ${selectedMembers.size} ä¸ªä¼šå‘˜å—ï¼Ÿ`)) return;
    
    let successCount = 0;
    for (const id of selectedMembers) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`/api/member/${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' });
            const result = await response.json();
            if (result.success) successCount++;
        } catch (error) {}
    }
    showToast('åˆ é™¤å®Œæˆ', `æˆåŠŸåˆ é™¤ ${successCount} ä¸ªä¼šå‘˜`);
    loadMembers(currentPage);
    loadStatistics();
}

function showAddModal() {
    document.getElementById('addTelegramId').value = '';
    document.getElementById('addUsername').value = '';
    document.getElementById('addReferrerId').value = '';
    document.getElementById('addBalance').value = '0';
    document.getElementById('addGroupLink').value = '';
    document.getElementById('addIsGroupBound').value = '0';
    document.getElementById('addIsBotAdmin').value = '0';
    document.getElementById('addIsJoinedUpline').value = '0';
    document.getElementById('addIsVip').value = '0';
    showModal('addModal');
}

async function saveMember() {
    const telegramId = document.getElementById('addTelegramId').value;
    if (!telegramId) {
        showToast('é”™è¯¯', 'è¯·è¾“å…¥ç”¨æˆ·ID', 'error');
        return;
    }
    
    const data = {
        telegram_id: parseInt(telegramId),
        username: document.getElementById('addUsername').value,
        referrer_id: document.getElementById('addReferrerId').value ? parseInt(document.getElementById('addReferrerId').value) : null,
        balance: parseFloat(document.getElementById('addBalance').value) || 0,
        group_link: document.getElementById('addGroupLink').value,
        is_group_bound: parseInt(document.getElementById('addIsGroupBound').value),
        is_bot_admin: parseInt(document.getElementById('addIsBotAdmin').value),
        is_joined_upline: parseInt(document.getElementById('addIsJoinedUpline').value),
        is_vip: parseInt(document.getElementById('addIsVip').value)
    };
    
    try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/member/add', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });
        const result = await response.json();
        if (result.success) {
            showToast('æˆåŠŸ', 'ä¼šå‘˜æ³¨å†ŒæˆåŠŸ');
            closeModal('addModal');
            loadMembers(currentPage);
            loadStatistics();
        } else {
            showToast('å¤±è´¥', result.message || 'æ³¨å†Œå¤±è´¥', 'error');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('é”™è¯¯', error.message, 'error');
    }
}

                        <option value="0" ${!currentMember.is_joined_upline ? 'selected' : ''}>å¦</option>

            </div>`;
        showModal('editModal');

async function saveEdit() {
    if (!currentMember) return;
    
    const data = {
        username: document.getElementById('editUsername').value,
        referrer_id: document.getElementById('editReferrerId').value ? parseInt(document.getElementById('editReferrerId').value) : null,
        balance: parseFloat(document.getElementById('editBalance').value),
        group_link: document.getElementById('editGroupLink').value,
        is_group_bound: parseInt(document.getElementById('editIsGroupBound').value),
        is_bot_admin: parseInt(document.getElementById('editIsBotAdmin').value),
        is_joined_upline: parseInt(document.getElementById('editIsJoinedUpline').value),
        is_vip: parseInt(document.getElementById('editIsVip').value)
    };
    
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`/api/member/${currentMember.telegram_id}`, {
            method: 'PUT',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });
        const result = await response.json();
        if (result.success) {
            showToast('ä¿å­˜æˆåŠŸ', 'ä¼šå‘˜ä¿¡æ¯å·²æ›´æ–°');
            closeModal('editModal');
            loadMembers(currentPage);
            loadStatistics();
        } else {
            showToast('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥', result.message, 'error');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('ä¿å­˜å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
    }
}


function toggleLevel(level) {
    const content = document.getElementById(`level-${level}-content`);
    const icon = document.getElementById(`icon-level-${level}`);
    if (content.style.display === 'none') {
        content.style.display = 'grid';
        icon.classList.remove('ti-chevron-right');
        icon.classList.add('ti-chevron-down');
    } else {
        content.style.display = 'none';
        icon.classList.remove('ti-chevron-down');
        icon.classList.add('ti-chevron-right');
    }
}

async function showGraph(telegramId) {
    try {
        console.log('å¼€å§‹åŠ è½½å›¾è°±æ•°æ®, telegramId:', telegramId);

        const response = await fetch(`/api/member/${telegramId}/graph`);
        console.log('APIå“åº”çŠ¶æ€:', response.status);

        if (!response.ok) {
            throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}: ${response.statusText}`);
        }
        const data = await response.json();
        console.log('APIè¿”å›çš„å®Œæ•´æ•°æ®:', data);

        // æ£€æŸ¥è¿”å›çš„æ•°æ®æ˜¯å¦æœ‰æ•ˆ
        if (!data || typeof data !== 'object') {
            throw new Error('å›¾è°±æ•°æ®æ ¼å¼é”™è¯¯');
        }

        // å®‰å…¨æ£€æŸ¥æ‰€æœ‰å…³é”®å±æ€§
        if (data.center === undefined) {
            console.warn('è­¦å‘Š: data.center æœªå®šä¹‰');
        }
        if (data.uplines === undefined) {
            console.warn('è­¦å‘Š: data.uplines æœªå®šä¹‰');
        }
        if (data.downlines === undefined) {
            console.warn('è­¦å‘Š: data.downlines æœªå®šä¹‰');
        }
        
        let html = '<div class="space-y-6">';
        
        // ä¸Šçº§é“¾
        html += '<div class="bg-blue-50 rounded-lg p-4">';
        html += '<h4 class="font-bold text-blue-800 mb-3 flex items-center gap-2"><i class="ti ti-arrow-up"></i> ä¸Šçº§é“¾</h4>';
        const uplines = data.uplines || data.upline || [];
        if (uplines && uplines.length > 0) {
            html += '<div class="space-y-2">';
            uplines.forEach((u, i) => {
                if (!u) return; // è·³è¿‡æ— æ•ˆæ•°æ®
                const levelName = i === 0 ? 'ä¸Šä¸€å±‚' : (i === 1 ? 'ä¸ŠäºŒå±‚' : `ä¸Š${i+1}å±‚`);
                const statusClass = u.is_valid ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700' : 'bg-red-100 text-red-700';
                const statusText = u.is_valid ? 'æ­£å¸¸' : 'å¼‚å¸¸';
                html += `<div class="flex items-center gap-3 bg-white rounded-lg p-3 border">
                    <span class="px-2 py-1 text-xs rounded bg-blue-100 text-blue-700 font-bold">${levelName}</span>
                    <span class="font-mono">${u.telegram_id || 'æœªçŸ¥'}</span>
                    <span class="text-indigo-600 font-medium">@${u.username || 'N/A'}</span>
                    <span class="px-2 py-0.5 text-xs rounded ${u.is_vip ? 'bg-amber-100 text-amber-700' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-500'}">${u.is_vip ? 'VIP' : 'æ™®é€š'}</span>
                    <span class="text-slate-500">ç›´æ¨:${u.direct_count || 0}</span>
                    <span class="text-slate-500">å›¢é˜Ÿ:${u.team_count || 0}</span>
                    <span class="px-2 py-0.5 text-xs rounded ${statusClass}">${statusText}</span>
                </div>`;
            });
            html += '</div>';
        } else {
            html += '<p class="text-slate-500">æ— ä¸Šçº§</p>';
        }
        html += '</div>';
        
        // å½“å‰ç”¨æˆ·
        html += '<div class="bg-indigo-100 rounded-lg p-4">';
        html += '<h4 class="font-bold text-indigo-800 mb-3 flex items-center gap-2"><i class="ti ti-user"></i> å½“å‰ä¼šå‘˜</h4>';
        const current = data.current || data.center;
        if (current) {
        html += `<div class="bg-white rounded-lg p-3 border-2 border-indigo-400">
            <div class="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <span class="font-mono text-lg">${current.telegram_id || 'æœªçŸ¥'}</span>
                    <span class="text-indigo-600 font-bold text-lg">@${current.username || 'N/A'}</span>
                    <span class="px-2 py-0.5 text-xs rounded ${current.is_vip ? 'bg-amber-100 text-amber-700' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-500'}">${current.is_vip ? 'VIP' : 'æ™®é€š'}</span>
                    <span class="text-emerald-600 font-bold">${current.balance || 0}U</span>
            </div>
        </div>`;
        } else {
            html += '<div class="bg-white rounded-lg p-3 border-2 border-red-400 text-red-600">æ— æ³•è·å–å½“å‰ç”¨æˆ·ä¿¡æ¯</div>';
        }
        html += '</div>';
        
        // ä¸‹çº§æˆå‘˜ï¼ˆå…¼å®¹æ–°æ—§APIï¼‰
        html += '<div class="bg-green-50 rounded-lg p-4">';
        html += '<h4 class="font-bold text-green-800 mb-3 flex items-center gap-2"><i class="ti ti-arrow-down"></i> ä¸‹çº§æˆå‘˜</h4>';
        
        // ä½¿ç”¨æ–°çš„APIæ ¼å¼ (data.downlines)
        let downlines = data.downlines || data.downline || [];

        // è½¬æ¢ä¸ºå±‚çº§åˆ†ç»„æ ¼å¼
        let downlineData = {};
        downlines.forEach(d => {
            const level = d.level || 1;
            if (!downlineData[level]) downlineData[level] = [];
            downlineData[level].push(d);
        });
        
        if (Object.keys(downlineData).length > 0) {
            const levels = Object.keys(downlineData).sort((a,b) => parseInt(a) - parseInt(b));
            levels.forEach(level => {
                const members = downlineData[level];
                if (members && members.length > 0) {
                    html += `<div class="mb-4">
                        <div class="text-sm font-bold text-green-700 mb-2 flex items-center gap-2 cursor-pointer hover:bg-green-100 p-2 rounded transition-colors" onclick="toggleLevel(${level})">
                            <i id="icon-level-${level}" class="ti ti-chevron-down text-lg"></i>
                            <span class="px-2 py-1 rounded bg-green-200">ç¬¬${level}å±‚</span>
                            <span class="text-slate-500">(${members.length}äºº)</span>
                        </div>
                        <div id="level-${level}-content" class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">`;
                    members.forEach(d => {
                        if (!d) return; // è·³è¿‡æ— æ•ˆæ•°æ®
                        const statusClass = (d.is_group_bound && d.is_bot_admin && d.is_joined_upline) ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700' : 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-700';
                        const statusText = (d.is_group_bound && d.is_bot_admin && d.is_joined_upline) ? 'æ­£å¸¸' : 'æœªå®Œæˆ';
                        html += `<div class="bg-white rounded-lg p-2 border text-xs">
                            <div class="flex items-center gap-1 flex-wrap">
                                <span class="font-mono">${d.telegram_id || 'æœªçŸ¥'}</span>
                                <span class="text-indigo-600 font-medium">@${d.username || 'N/A'}</span>
                            </div>
                            <div class="flex items-center gap-1 mt-1">
                                <span class="px-1 py-0.5 rounded ${d.is_vip ? 'bg-amber-100 text-amber-700' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-500'}">${d.is_vip ? 'VIP' : 'æ™®é€š'}</span>
                                <span class="text-slate-500">ç›´:${d.direct_count || 0}</span>
                                <span class="text-slate-500">å›¢:${d.team_count || 0}</span>
                                <span class="px-1 py-0.5 rounded ${statusClass}">${statusText}</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>`;
                    });
                    html += '</div></div>';
                }
            });
        } else {
            html += '<p class="text-slate-500">æš‚æ— ä¸‹çº§</p>';
        }
        html += '</div>';
        
        html += '</div>';
        
        document.getElementById('graphContent').innerHTML = html;
        showModal('graphModal');
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
    }
}

async function deleteMember(telegramId, username) {
    if (!confirm(`ç¡®å®šè¦åˆ é™¤ä¼šå‘˜ ${username} å—ï¼Ÿ`)) return;
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`/api/member/${telegramId}`, { method: 'DELETE' });
        const result = await response.json();
        if (result.success) {
            showToast('åˆ é™¤æˆåŠŸ', 'ä¼šå‘˜å·²åˆ é™¤');
            loadMembers(currentPage);
            loadStatistics();
        }
    } catch (error) {
        showToast('åˆ é™¤å¤±è´¥', error.message, 'error');
    }
}

function showModal(id) { document.getElementById(id).classList.add('show'); }
function closeModal(id) { document.getElementById(id).classList.remove('show'); }

});

<script>
        // è·å–telegram_idï¼Œå¦‚æœæœªå®šä¹‰åˆ™ä½¿ç”¨é»˜è®¤å€¼
        let telegramId;
        try {
            telegramId = {{ telegram_id | tojson }};
            if (telegramId === null || telegramId === undefined) {
                telegramId = 0;
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('è·å–telegram_idå¤±è´¥:', e);
            telegramId = 0;
        }

        console.log('åˆå§‹åŒ–telegramId:', telegramId);
        
        async function loadGraph() {
            try {
                // æ˜¾ç¤ºåŠ è½½çŠ¶æ€
                document.getElementById('centerContent').innerHTML = '<p class="text-slate-400">æ­£åœ¨åŠ è½½æ•°æ®...</p>';
                document.getElementById('uplinesContent').innerHTML = '<p class="text-slate-400">æ­£åœ¨åŠ è½½...</p>';
                document.getElementById('downlinesContent').innerHTML = '<p class="text-slate-400">æ­£åœ¨åŠ è½½...</p>';

                const apiUrl = `/api/member/${telegramId}/graph`;
                console.log('è¯·æ±‚API:', apiUrl);

                const res = await fetch(apiUrl);
                console.log('APIå“åº”çŠ¶æ€:', res.status);

                if (!res.ok) {
                    throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}: ${res.statusText}`);
                }

                const data = await res.json();
                console.log('APIè¿”å›æ•°æ®:', data);

                // æ£€æŸ¥æ•°æ®ç»“æ„
                if (!data || typeof data !== 'object') {
                    throw new Error('APIè¿”å›æ•°æ®æ ¼å¼é”™è¯¯');
                }

                // è·å–ä¸­å¿ƒç”¨æˆ·ä¿¡æ¯
                const center = data.center;
                if (!center || typeof center !== 'object') {
                    throw new Error('ç”¨æˆ·ä¸­å¿ƒæ•°æ®ä¸å­˜åœ¨');
                }

                console.log('ä¸­å¿ƒç”¨æˆ·:', center);
                
                // æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸­å¿ƒç”¨æˆ·
                const centerHtml = `
                    <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                        <div>
                            <p class="text-lg font-bold text-slate-900">@${center.username || 'æœªçŸ¥'}</p>
                            <p class="text-sm text-slate-600">ID: ${center.telegram_id || 'æœªçŸ¥'}</p>
                        </div>
                        <div class="text-right">
                            <p class="text-sm text-slate-600">ä½™é¢: <span class="font-bold text-indigo-600">${center.balance || 0} U</span></p>
                            <p class="text-sm text-slate-600">ç´¯è®¡: <span class="font-bold text-green-600">${center.total_earned || 0} U</span></p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mt-3">
                        <span class="inline-flex items-center px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-sm font-semibold ${center.is_vip ? 'bg-purple-100 text-purple-700' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-600'}">
                            ${center.is_vip ? 'ğŸ’ VIPä¼šå‘˜' : 'âŒ éVIP'}
                        </span>
                    </div>
                `;
                document.getElementById('centerContent').innerHTML = centerHtml;
                
                // æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸Šçº§
                const uplines = data.uplines || [];
                console.log('ä¸Šçº§æ•°é‡:', uplines.length);

                if (uplines && uplines.length > 0) {
                    const uplinesHtml = uplines.map(u => {
                        if (!u || typeof u !== 'object') return '';
                        return `
                        <div class="flex items-center gap-3 p-3 bg-slate-50 rounded-lg border border-slate-200 hover:bg-indigo-50 hover:border-indigo-300 transition">
                                <span class="flex-shrink-0 w-12 h-12 rounded-full bg-indigo-100 flex items-center justify-center font-bold text-indigo-700">L${u.level || '?'}</span>
                            <div class="flex-1">
                                    <p class="font-semibold text-slate-900">@${u.username || 'æœªçŸ¥'}</p>
                                    <p class="text-xs text-slate-500">ID: ${u.telegram_id || 'æœªçŸ¥'}</p>
                            </div>
                            <div class="flex gap-2">
                                <span class="text-lg" title="${u.is_vip ? 'VIP' : 'éVIP'}">${u.is_vip ? 'ğŸ’' : 'âŒ'}</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        `;
                    }).join('');
                    document.getElementById('uplinesContent').innerHTML = uplinesHtml;
                } else {
                    document.getElementById('uplinesContent').innerHTML = '<p class="text-slate-400">æš‚æ— ä¸Šçº§</p>';
                }
                
                // æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸‹çº§
                const downlines = data.downlines || [];
                console.log('ä¸‹çº§æ•°é‡:', downlines.length);

                if (downlines && downlines.length > 0) {
                    // æŒ‰å±‚çº§åˆ†ç»„
                    const levels = {};
                    downlines.forEach(d => {
                        if (!d || typeof d !== 'object') return;
                        const lvl = d.level || 1;
                        if (!levels[lvl]) levels[lvl] = [];
                        levels[lvl].push(d);
                    });
                    
                    const downlinesHtml = Object.keys(levels).sort((a,b) => a-b).map(level => {
                        const members = levels[level];
                        if (!members || members.length === 0) return '';

                        const membersHtml = members.map(d => {
                            if (!d || typeof d !== 'object') return '';
                            return `
                                    <div class="flex items-center gap-3 p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded-lg border border-slate-200 text-sm">
                                        <div class="flex-1">
                                        <p class="font-semibold text-slate-900">@${d.username || 'æœªçŸ¥'}</p>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="flex gap-1">
                                            <span title="${d.is_vip ? 'VIP' : 'éVIP'}">${d.is_vip ? 'ğŸ’' : 'âŒ'}</span>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            `;
                        }).join('');

                        return `
                            <div class="mb-4">
                                <h3 class="text-sm font-bold text-slate-700 mb-2">ç¬¬${level}å±‚ (${members.length}äºº)</h3>
                                <div class="space-y-2">
                                    ${membersHtml}
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        `;
                    }).join('');

                    document.getElementById('downlinesContent').innerHTML = downlinesHtml;
                } else {
                    document.getElementById('downlinesContent').innerHTML = '<p class="text-slate-400">æš‚æ— ä¸‹çº§</p>';
                }
                
                console.log('å›¾è°±åŠ è½½å®Œæˆ');

            } catch (error) {
                console.error('å›¾è°±åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:', error);

                // æ˜¾ç¤ºé”™è¯¯ä¿¡æ¯
                const errorHtml = `<div class="text-red-500 p-4 bg-red-50 rounded-lg border border-red-200">
                    <h3 class="font-bold mb-2">æ•°æ®åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥</h3>
                    <p class="text-sm">${error.message}</p>
                    <p class="text-xs mt-2 text-gray-500">è¯·åˆ·æ–°é¡µé¢é‡è¯•æˆ–è”ç³»ç®¡ç†å‘˜</p>
                </div>`;

                document.getElementById('centerContent').innerHTML = errorHtml;
                document.getElementById('uplinesContent').innerHTML = '';
                document.getElementById('downlinesContent').innerHTML = '';
            }
        }
        
        // é¡µé¢åŠ è½½å®Œæˆåæ‰§è¡Œ
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            console.log('é¡µé¢åŠ è½½å®Œæˆï¼Œå¼€å§‹åŠ è½½å›¾è°±æ•°æ®');
loadGraph();

<!-- Toast -->
<div id="toast" class="fixed top-6 right-6 z-50 transform transition-all duration-300 translate-x-full opacity-0">
    <div class="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-xl border p-4 flex items-center gap-3 min-w-[300px]">
        <div id="toast-icon"></div>
        <div>
            <div id="toast-title" class="font-semibold text-slate-900"></div>

        </div>

<script>
(function() {
    let page = 1, search = '', pages = 1;
    
    // Toast
    function toast(title, msg, ok) {
        const t = document.getElementById('toast');
        document.getElementById('toast-icon').innerHTML = ok 
            ? '<div class="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-green-50 flex items-center justify-center"><i class="ti ti-check text-green-600"></i></div>'
            : '<div class="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-red-50 flex items-center justify-center"><i class="ti ti-x text-red-600"></i></div>';
        document.getElementById('toast-title').textContent = title;
        document.getElementById('toast-msg').textContent = msg;
        t.classList.remove('translate-x-full', 'opacity-0');
        setTimeout(() => t.classList.add('translate-x-full', 'opacity-0'), 3000);
    }
    
    // åŠ è½½æ•°æ®
    async function load() {
        let url = `/api/earnings?page=${page}`;
        if (search) url += `&search=${encodeURIComponent(search)}`;
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch(url);
            const data = await res.json();
            
            const tbody = document.getElementById('table-body');
            const empty = document.getElementById('empty');
            
            if (!data.records || data.records.length === 0) {
                tbody.innerHTML = '';
                empty.classList.remove('hidden');
            } else {
                empty.classList.add('hidden');
                tbody.innerHTML = data.records.map(item => {
                    return `<tr class="hover:bg-slate-50">
                        <td class="px-6 py-4 text-slate-500">#${item.id}</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4"><div class="font-medium text-slate-900">@${item.username || 'N/A'}</div><div class="text-xs text-slate-500">ID: ${item.member_id || 'N/A'}</div></td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4 font-bold text-emerald-600">+${item.amount} U</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4 text-slate-600">${item.upgraded_user_name || '-'}</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4 text-slate-600">${item.description || '-'}</td>
                        <td class="px-6 py-4 text-slate-500 text-xs">${item.create_time}</td>
                    </tr>`;
                }).join('');
            }
            
            document.getElementById('total').textContent = data.total || 0;
            document.getElementById('page-num').textContent = data.page || 1;
            pages = data.pages || 1;
            document.getElementById('prev-btn').disabled = page <= 1;
            document.getElementById('next-btn').disabled = page >= pages;
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('Load error:', e);
            toast('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥', 'ç½‘ç»œé”™è¯¯', false);
        }
    }
    
    // æœç´¢æŒ‰é’®
    document.getElementById('search-btn').addEventListener('click', function() {
        search = document.getElementById('search-input').value.trim();
        page = 1;
        load();
    });
    
    // å›è½¦æœç´¢
    document.getElementById('search-input').addEventListener('keypress', function(e) {
        if (e.key === 'Enter') {
            e.preventDefault();
            search = this.value.trim();
            page = 1;
            load();
        }
    });
    
    // åˆ†é¡µ
    document.getElementById('prev-btn').addEventListener('click', () => { if (page > 1) { page--; load(); } });
    document.getElementById('next-btn').addEventListener('click', () => { if (page < pages) { page++; load(); } });
    
    // åˆå§‹åŠ è½½
    load();
})();
</script>
